013



Kwanaki biyu kenan rabonda tasa daddynta ido, sanda zata fito bayanan bata kuma sanin dawowarshi.

Yau ranar Alhamis, as usual tadawo Daga aikine agajiye. 
Dakyar ta iya kai motar wajen parking tayi parking.
A kasalance ta fito ta rufe motar.

Wata mota tagani a parking space din Wanda ba tasu bace.

Tsayawa tayi tana kallon motar taba tunanin to ta wanene?

Wucewa tayi ta murda kofan falon tashiga da sallama.

Tarin dataji Anayi ba qauqautawa ne, yasata jin ta wartsake nan take.

"Dad?.." Tafada idanunta waje.

Da sauri tanufi part dinshi tana kwala mishi kira.

Murda kofar tayi tashiga, Turus tayi tareda saurin rufe bakinta da tafin hannu.

Dad ne kwance yana tari kamar na fitar rai ga doctor ya duqufa kanshi yana qoqarin shawo kan tarin.

"Daddy!" Tafada da qarfi tayi wurgi da handbag dinta taruga wajenshi.

Kamoshi tayi tana kuka ganin yadda yake tarin Duk ilahirin jikinshi rawa na rawa.

"Nashiga uku daddy, doctor what's happening to my daddy?" Tafada cikin kuka sosai.

"Please miss Saudart kiyi hqr kifita"

"No!" Tafada tana qara rugumoshi tana kuka sosai.

"Please kinaso muyi loosing dinshi? Kibari nayi aikina"

Jin hakan yasata janyewa Amma still tana kuka.

"Kifita please, kijira waje, komai zaiyi daidai insha Allah"

Badon tasoba tafita tasamu wata kujera ta zauna tana kuka.

Meke damun daddynta? Dama bayada lfy? Tun yaushema yafara rashin lfy? Anya kau ta kyautama kanta? Ace mahaifinta suna gida daya Amma harya kwanta ciwo bata saniba?

Haka taita jerama kanta tambayoyi tana kuka.

Bayan kusan mintuna ashirin sai gashi doctorn yafito yana yarfe gumi.

Da sauri tamiqe tana kallonshi

"Doctor ya yake? Is he fine? Please tell me he is, please"

"Miss Saudart, ki kwantar da hankalinki please, zauna zamuyi magana"

Zama tayi hawaye nabin kuncinta

"Saudart garin yaya kuka barshi har yakai wannan stage din batareda kun kaishi asibitiba?"

Kan Saudart yasake kullewa

"Doctor meke damunshi ne? Wlh bansan baya lfy ba" 

"Really? Kuma kuna kwana under roof daya ace bakida masaniya akan lfyanshi?"

Kasa amsawa tayi sai kuka.

"Well am sorry, Amma daddynki yakamu da ciwon zuciya"

Waro dara daran idanunta tayi tana toshe bakinta da hannu tana girgiza kai unbelievably

"No, it can't be" 

"Yes miss Saudart, daddynki yakamu da ciwon zuciya sanadin damuwa, damuwa tamishi yawa har yayi sanadin stressing din zuciyarshi yanzu haka gab take da bugawa"

"No!!" Saikuma tafashe da kuka abin tausayi.

"Nashiga uku ni Saudatu, daddy idan katafi kabarni ya zanyi?"

"Bazai tafiba insha Allah idan kuna kiyayewa, Ku kiyayi 6atamishi rai, Ku dinga yimashi abinda zai faranta mishi, sbd next time yasamu wani attack din sai Allah"

Kuka take afujanjan, badai akan wannan auren contract dinba yakamu da ciwon zuciya ba? Badai tasoshi gaba yan banki sukayi ba? Ita Saudart ina hankalinta yatafi ta za6i tayi nisa da daddynta a lokacin dayafi buqatarta? Kaico.

"Ga magunguna can na ajiye a bedside locker akwai prescription dinsu ajiki, a dinga kulawa da maganinshi and I repeat aguji 6ata ranshi"

Daga haka yayi mata sallama yafice.

Ta dade zaune awajen tana kuka sannan ta lalla6a ta tashi tashiga dakin daddyn.

Ahankali taqaraso wajenshi tana kallonshi, kukane yakusan kufce mata tayi saurin dade baki don karta tadashi.

Zama tayi gabanshi ta riqo hannunshi tana murzawa ahankali.

"Dad ka yafemin, nakasa share maka hawaye ka yafemin" tafada cikin muryar kuka.

Saida tayi mai isanta sannan ta share hawayenta.

"Daddy insha Allah bazan ta6a bijirema ba, badai akan bashin bankiba? Insha Allah nizan sharema hawayenka.
Gobe insha Allah zanje in saka bakery na kasuwa, banga amfaninshi ba idan inada damar siyar wa in taimakekaba. Insha Allah damuwar ka tazo qarshe"

Don tsabar takaici jiyayi kamar yabuga uban tsaki Daga inda yake kwance.

Wai wacce iriyar yarinya ce wannan mai kunnen qashi? Wato har lanbon ciwonma bazai sata Amincewa da qudurinshiba? Tsaki yaja azuciyarshi, jiyake kamar yatashi yaita kifeta da Mari.
Wai bakery? Ana batun arziqi waketa tsinannen bakery can.

Haka taita sabbatunta shikau sai qumuwa yake da takaici Saidai ba halin yako motsa.

Aka ta kwana tana kulada Alhaji

Washegari kau tayi waya dawani wanda tasani akan maganar siyarda bakery dinta.

Saidai me? Duk inda akaje Saidai ayimasu tayin wulaqanci.

Tun tana daukar abin wasa har abun yafara bata tsoro, kwata kwata highest din tayin 5million.

Sosai tashiga damuwa, Duk inda akaje Saidai suce ai yanzu abubuwa sun rage daraja, corona virus.


Abinda batasaniba, daddynta ne keda sa hannu awannan abin, shi yasa akebin kwakwafinta Duk inda taje siyar wa saisu saye mutanen akan suyimata tayin wulaqanci.


Saidai naci da taurin kan Saudart yaqi bari ta hqr.

Ganin wankin hula na naiman kaishi dare yasashi watarana burkuce mata, aman jini yadinga yi ba kakkautawa.

Hankalin Saudart yatashi ainun idan banda kuka babu abinda take.

Koda takira doctor fada yayita mata kan idan Alhaji yamutu itace.

Haka taita kuka ganin dai babu sarki sai Allah tafara sabbatu.


"Wlh nayarda, nayarda zanyi auren, please kace yatashi"

Saura kadan Alhajin yabuga tsalle don dadi.

"At last, at long last" yaita nannatawa aranshi.


Tofa? Burin Alhaji shamsu fah yacika, zaizamo sirukin Sir A.A 😅

Cikin kwana biyu ya warke sumul sai nan nan yakeda Saudart, itako kwata kwata tarasa abinda kemata dadi.

She can't believe ta yarda da AUREN KWANGILA da wannan monster dinba.

Jitake Dama mutuwa tayi tahuta.

Ada batasan qiyayyaba, ko wuqa aka samata awuya akace tafadi maqiyinta daya bata iyawa.

Amma yanzu qiyayar datakema Ashraf bata misaltuwa, shine sanadin rugujewar farincikinta, shine silan rushewar burinta na aure mutu-ka-raba, uwa uba shine silan sa6awa ubangijinta.
She soo much hate him. With passion.



MONDAY


Su Alhaji shamsu yau ko barci ba'a komaba Bayan asuba, sai shirin ganawa da A.A ake.

Yau za'ayi signing din contract din auren...✍

014





Kwankwasa kofarta da'akayi ne ya tsaidata Daga shafa man datake.

Hijabi tazura tanufi kofar tabude.

Fuskar daddynta yayi mata maraba washe da fara'a.

Itama washe fuskarta tayi tana matsawa gefe don yashigo.

"A'a? Inyee? Dad wannan hadewa haka kamar wanda zaya gana da president?"

Dariya yayi sannan yace
"Ai wanda zamu gana dashi dinma yakai President dinma koma yafi sbd shi gumin kanshi yakeci bawai na al'umma ba, besides yanaga baki shiryaba?"

"Wlh Dad yanzu zan shirya, ai duka yanzu eight fa, inada sauran time"

"Bamuda time shalele, we ought to be there by 9"

"Wai Dad sai cewa 'mu' kake, dawa dawa?"

"Ni da ke mana"

"Tofa? Fita zamuyi Dama?"

"Mtcheew, kin cika shirme shalele, nufinki bakisan yau zamuje signing din contract dinba?"

Sororo tayi tana kallonshi

"Contract?"

"Mtcheew, Wai meke damunki ne, nufinki bakisan yau ake signing din AUREN KWANGILARKU BA"

Gabanta ne yafadi, dagaske kenan aurennan will push through?

"Kinyi shiru?"

"Dad yanzu fisabillilah kai zakaje shi bazai zoba, Dad indirectly zuwa tallana fa kake"

"Ya ilahi Saudart, don girman Allah kibar maido hannun agogo baya, Nike nema wajenshi so nizan je" yafada cikin Fushi.

"To Allah ya tsare, nikam bani zuwa, kuma please daddy karkace zaka tilastani don Dama auren bawani kwanta min yayiba" tafada tana zama gefen gado ta cigaba da shafa kafanta mai.

"Shalele ni kikema haka don kinga ina Neman Abu awajenki?"

Kamar wanda yacema tafara.

Aikau saita fashe da kuka, harda shesheka kamar wanda akayima tsinannan duka.

Sakin baki Alhaji yayi yana kallonta.

Ganin abin nata bana qarewa bane, saiya zauna kusada ita yajata jikinshi ya hau rarrashi.

"Shikenan Shikenan, Basai kinje ba, kibar kukan haka, kiyi shiru please"

Dakyar yasamu tayi shiru sannan yafice yatafi shi kadai.

Tashi tayi Bayan fitarshi.
"Ca6di! Wlh bana fatan wani Abu yasake hadani da wannan jerk din, tsinemin akayi?"

A gurguje ta shirya itama tafice bakery dinta.







***********************************************




"No way! Wannan Abu mu uku yashafa, don haka mu uku zamuyi sign kamar yadda kagani a paper"

"Nasani Mr A.A Amma kamar yadda na fadama bata jindadi ne, da daita zanzo"

"To sai abari saita warke sai Ayi, yanzu kai kayi sign din naka, idan ta warware saitazo tayi nata sannan zakaji alert" inji Ashraf da yake ganinma Alhaji shamsu yayi mugun raina mishi wayau.

Shiru Alhaji shamsu yayi yana tunani

"Look is not as if ina tilastama neba, idan wannan abin bazai yiwuba abarshi please"

"No..no bahaka vane Mr A.A, kawo inyi signing, insha Allah zuwa gobe idan ta warware zatazo tayi nata"

Yafada yana amsar paper, ya karanta sharuddan kamar dai yadda Dama yasani sannan yasa hannu wajen da yakamata yasa.

"Gashi insha Allah gobe zataso" injishi yana miqama Sadeeq  da tundazun ko A bece ba.

"To Allah yakaimu" inji sadeeq while Ashraf yawani lumshe idanu kamar maijin barci.


Bayan tafiyarshi sadeeq ya kalli Ashraf da idanunshi ke lumshe haryanzu.

"Wai! Gaskiya yarinyar nan yar jin kai ce,komai saitaja aji?"

"Get out!"

"Toni menayi kuma?" Yafada cikin dariya.

"Kasan Allah ubanka zanci, nace out!!"

Harara ya galla mashi sannan yafita yana gunguni.






*************************************
WASHEGARI



A kasalance take shirinta nayau, haryanzu abinda yafaru tsakaninta da Dad jiya yaqi sakinta.

Sosai jiya daddy ya burkuce mata jiya don tace baza taje tayi sign ba.

A jiya tasan dayan 6aren daddynta, don be raga mataba tatass yamata abin ba dadinji.

Bata ta6a tunanin akan dan Abu irin wannan dad zai mata tijara irin najiya ba.


Don dole ta amince zataje don bazata iya da masifar Dad ba.



Shirya wa tayi cikin wani sky blue Arabian gown ta nade kanta da gyallen rigar sannan ta rataye side bag dinta sky blue.

Masha Allah tayi kyau musanmman data kwama baqin shade a idanu mai taken NO RESPECT.

saukowa tayi ahankali, a dining ta ga dad zaune yana kari, kallo daya yayi mata ya dauke kai.

Murmushi tayi taqaraso wajenshi tana cire glass din idonta.

"Good morning dad"

"Morning" ya amsa kamar mai ciwon baki.

Jawo plate din gabanshi tayi tasaka fork itama tanaci.

Ci kanki bece daitaba.

Ganin haka yasa ta dago ta kalleshi a marairaice.

"Dad!"

Shiru

"Dad don Allah kayi hqr, fushin ka agareni masifa ce"

Nanma shiru.

"Please Dad Kaga Daga nanma can na nufa, kayi hqr"

Dukda yaji dadi Amma ko nunawa beyiba saima banza dayayi daita.

Kuka tafara ahankali, saurin dagowa yayi tareda jawoya ajiki yana rarrashi don ga yadda tayi kyau dinnan beson tayi kuka kwalliyar ta6aci🤔

"It ok sweetheart, ya isa please, na haqura"

Shima saida yasha fama sannan ta hqr.

Har mota ya rakata yanata samata albarka.

Shiga tayi ta dagamashi hannu sannan ta tada motar ta fice cikin tuqi mai burgewa.

Naunnauyan ajiyar zuciya Alhaji yasaki yana girgiza kai, Saudart? Hmn halinta sai ita.







Tuqi take tana saqe saqe, she can't believe Wai zuwa zatayi tayi signing din aurenta da wanda kwata kwata besan darajar mutane ba.

Lallai, aikau yau she won't take shit, idan yayimata ramawa zatayi don ba tsoronshi ba takeji.

Tsaki taja, yanzu me zeta cemishi idan taje? Nazo signing din contract din auren mu? Mezai dauketa? Mai binshi din dagaske? Gashi tagama ikirarin bekai standard din mallakarta dadai da second dayaba, nezai dauketa yanzu?

"Kai wlh daddy kagama dani!" Tafada tana dukan steering 

Saudart Nada sanyin hali Saidai bata jurar wulaqanci, Duk yadda kuke daita ka nemi raina mata wayau yanzu kunyi sama Ku tiqo qasa.

Tanada hqr haka kuma tanada zafi sosai, shiyasa ko a qawaye shakkar 6atamata rai ake.


Danna hancin motarta tayi cikin harabar company din Bayan an wangale mata gate din.

Yau company din bewani yimata kyau ba.

Tafi minti biyar amotar takasa fitowa kawai fargabar shiga take, dayake ruwa ruwace har hawaye sunfara kwanciya a kwarin idanunta.

"Dad ka gama dani, ka gama dani" haka taita nanatawa.

Saida ta tattaro sauran jarumtarta sannan ta bude murfin kofar tafito ahankali....✍


Sorry nasan yayi kadan ba chaji🙏

015






Maida murfin kofar tayi tarufe sannan ta kulle motar.

Zaro baqin shade dinta tayi ta qwama a fuska wannan yakusan rufe Rabin fuskar sannan ta gyara zaman side bag dinta.
Ahankali cikin wani taku tanufi main entrance din.

Sanitizing din hannunta tayi sannan ta shiga ciki.

Direct elevator tanufa don ta riqe number floor din.

Cikin yan daqiqu abin yatsaya alamun anzo.

Ahankali tasanyo kafa tafito elevator din gabanta na bugun uku uku.

Allah yasani dauriya kawai take don zuciyarta fall take da fargaba.

Kamar kwanaki, Helen nanan mazauninta anci gayu cikin Riga da 6ingil din skirt, ga tulin gashin doki data tilama kai anmata style din baby face dashi.

Fuska a tamke ta qaraso wajen wanda qamshin turarenta ne ya fargar da Helen zuwanta.

Gaban Helen ne yafadi datayi tozali da wata unique super duper cutie, dukda shigarta simple ce ba qaramin kyau tayiba, gashi bawani kwalliya tayiba Amma kyan datayi baya misaltuwa.

"Is your boss around?" Inji Saudart cikin tsantseni.

"Yy..yes"

"Ok? Tell him yayi baquwa"

Tafada tana zama kan daya Daga kujerun wajen ta Dora kafa daya bisa daya.

Shiru kamar bazata tafiba, saikuma tatuna da haduwarsu na ranan, dan haka ta tashi tanufi office din.

"Yes? Come in" inji sadeeq dake tareda Ashraf yana nunamishi wani project dazakuyi presenting a wani meeting.

Helen ce tashigo jiki a sanyaye.

Gaishesu tafarayi sannan tace "sir kayi baquwa?"

"Who?"

"I don't know her name Amma seems Sir sadeeq yasanta"

Kallon juna sadeeq da Ashraf sukayi

"Ni?"

"Yes sir, wannan lady din ta ranan?"

Waro idanu yayi

"OMG!she's here, Alhaji shamsu's daughter, she made it at last" inji sadeeq cikin murna.

Kunya da takaici Yakama Ashraf, ji yadda yake Neman zubda mashi aji gaban wannan arniyar?

"Je kice tashigo" inji sadeeq da bemasan Ashraf nayi ba.

Juyawa tayi a ladabce

'Alhaji shamsu's daughter? Dama diyarshi ce?' Abinda yaita yawo azuciyarta kenan.


Yadda ta barta haka ta taddata sai wani kada kafaffu take ahankali.

"Kina iya shiga" inji Helen tana mata wani kallo marar fassara.

Ko a jikinta, ta tashi cikin nutsuwa ta gyara zaman kayanta sannan tanufi office din.

Ahankali ta bubbuga sau uku, sadeeq ne zaije ya bude mata Ashraf ya riqo hannunshi.

"Dan ubanka idan wannan rawar kan zakayiman zan koraka, idiot"

Sake bubbugowa akayi, ganin Ashraf Beda niyyar amsawa yasa sadeeq kware baki yana cewa
"Come in"

Ajiyar zuciya tasaki sannan ta runtse idanunta ta murda kofar ahankali, tashige.


"Ya subhanalillah!" Inji sadeeq cikin zuciya dayayi tozali da Saudart.

"Wow! Ta hadu ta hadu ta hadu!!!" Duk a zuciya yake zancenshi azahiri kuwa murmushi yake mata.

Shikau gogan kamar yadda kuka zata kanshi nakan system din gabanshi.

Sallama tayi ciki ciki, amsawa sadeeq yayi cikin fara'a yana mata iso.

Ashraf kamar ya shaqeshi don takaicin yadda yake wani rawar kafa.

A yangace tanufo kujerar da sadeeq yaja mata idanunta akan Ashraf Amma kasancewar baqin glass na idanunta ba'a ganewa.

Zama tayi ahankali sannan ta Dora kafa daya bisa daya.

"Ok boss, zan tafi in ida arrangement din" inji sadeeq yana tattara files din.

'What?' Yafada azuciyarshi, Amma mugun dan air ne sadeeq, nufinshi barinsu zaiyi su kadai.

Be ankaraba yaji qarar rufewar kofa alamun harya fita.


Wani irin shiru office din yadauka, itama kanta Saudart bataso tafiyar sadeeq ba don da niyyarta ta tambayi ina file din wajenshi tayi sign tafice don vataso ko kalma daya ya hadata da Ashraf.

Kusan mintuna biyar Amma shiru babu wanda ya motsa cikinsu, shi yana danne danne a system, ita tana shafe shafe a waya.

Minti biyar...Goma...Sha biyar Amma still ba wanda ya motsa.

Kowanne jira yake dan uwanshi yafara motsi.

Saudart takaici kamar tayi kuka, saitayi kamar tayimashi magana saikuma tafasa.

Shima hakan take a wajenshi, jiyake kamar yayi me?

(Ni Duk nafisu jin takaici, Wai wannan wane irin wulaqanci ne zasu barni sagale da Biro a hannu😠)


Ganin wankin hula na naiman kaita dare yasata motsawa, ahankali cikin yanga mai tattare da jin haushi tace
"Bani paper din inyi sign, Inada abinyi"

Murmushi Ashraf yayi cikin zuciyarshi, at last ta karaya.

Dago sharp cat eyes dinshi yayi ya doramata su a karo na farko tunda tashigo.

Ko seconds biyu beyiba yakuma dauke kai yacigaba da danne dannenshi.

Kutt! Lallai ma

Tashi tayi da niyyar ficewa don bazata iya jure wulaqancin shiba.

"Kina fita deal cancelled" yafada still hankalinshi kan computer

Dakatawa tayi zuciyarta na suya, gaskiya Dad yagama daita, wannan wulaqancin har ina.

Juyowa tayi tana kallonshi Jitake kamar ta rufeshi da duka.

"Look mallam inada abubuwan yi, let me sign the damn paper and leave"

Dagowa yayi Daga system din tareda komawa yayi balancing sosai a kujerar kamar irin dan sarkinnan.


Zubamata cat eyes dinshi yayi ya qureta da kallo.
Dukda glass din idanunta sun kareta Amma hakan be hanata jin tsinin idanunshi ba akanta.

"The paper?!" Tafada tsakankanin haqora cikin jin haushi don ko motsawa beyi yawani zubamata na mujiya.

"Paper? Which paper?" Ya tambaya cikin isa.

"Wanda kayi blackmailing din Dad na dashi mana, kabani inyi signing inyi tafiyata"

"Ba haka dad dinki yayi sadda yazo jiyaba, he begged for it, so kema ki roqa idan kinaso idan kuma bakiso?.." Saiya Daga kafadu sama alamun fine🤷‍♂



Shiru tayi tana kallonshi unbelievable, ta roqa? Yadda daddynta ya roqa? Kenan daddy strooping low yayi ya roqeshi? Innalillahi Dad yagama da ita.

Hawaye taji yana naiman saukomata, ga wani nauyi da zuciyarta tayi.

Qoqarin maida hawayen take don bataso yaga saukarsu yayinda tsanarshi sai qara farashi yake azuciyarshi.

"Miss shamsu, kina 6atamin time, beg me to marry you" yafada yana jindadin moment din don yasan ba qaramin wulaqanci yake shufka mataba.

Yasan babu yadda za'ayi tayi rejecting dinshi ko don daddynta, don Duk yadda akayi harta yarda yanada masaniya akai kuma yasan yanzuma forcing dinta Alhaji shamsu yayi hartazo.

Lumshe idanu Saudart tayi tana qoqarin saita muryarta

"Look, you don't have the idea of  how I hate you, stop pushing it, give the paper let me sign and leave, am suffocating here" tafada muryarta nadan cracking.

Tashi tsaye yayi ya tako ya zagayo gabanta cikin takun qasaita.

"Really? Kin tsaneni Amma kikazo Neman aurena? Wannan wacce iriyar tsana ce"

Hadiye wani Abu daya toshemata maqoshi tayi kafin tace
"Ba aurenka nazo nemaba, albarka mahaifi nazo nema don nasan darajarshi da matsayinshi if not ko sanin da wanzuwarka bazan yiba bare ko kallo ka isheni" tafada idanunta na qara durar ruwa.

"Then ki nemi albarkar dakyau, kiyi biyyaya gareni kamar yadda uban naki yayi, beg!" Ya ida zancen cikin rad'a


Kasa riqe hawayen tayi, saurin kauda kai gefe tayi don karyagansu.
 Jitake kamar tamutu don takaici.

Murmushin gefen baki yayi na mugunta ganin tana hawaye, Dama ya dauki alwashin saita raina kanta haduwarsu nagaba.

"Kinada minti daya kacal kiyi abinda yakawo ki ki fitarmin office don numfashinama sarqewa yake saboda odour"

Lumshe idanu tayi tana qara bama hawayenta damar gangara.

Shiru tayi atsaye still idanunta lumshe.

"10 seconds to go" yafada yana kallon agogo Bayan yakoma yayi balancing a kujera yana kallon yadda take hawaye.

Jan hanci tayi sannan ta goge fuskarta da hanki.

"Mr A.A kabani paper inyi signing.... Please" tafada tana sake lumshe idanunta tacikin glass.

Wani dadi Ashraf yaji jin tace please.
Amma saiya wani dago yana kallonta.

"Ban jiba come again"

Kuka takeso tayi Amma ta dake.
"Nace kabani paper inyi signing please"

"Beg with Hausa" yafada yana enjoying din moment din.

"Dan Allah..."

Murmushi yasaki na gefen baki sannan ya taso yasake zagayowa wajenta.

"In taimaka miki in baki?"

Wasu sabbin hawaye suka sake gangaro mata.

"Ehh" ta amsa murya na rawa

"Ehh what?" Yafada yana kafeta da idanu fuskarshi fall murmushin mugunta

"Ehh...Sir"

Furzar da iska yayi yana lumshe idanu cikin jindadi sannan ya budesu akanta.

Kanta na sadde Kasa hawaye na diga zuciyarta na wani irin zafi.

"Yanzu kinsan koni wanene?" Ya tambaya

"Yes"

"Yes what?"

"Yes sir" tafada tana girgiza kai ahankali don takaici.

"Yakamata kisan gabama da gabanta, nafi qarfin cakuri cici irinki, kamar yadda nafada abaya wutsiyar raqumi tayi nesa da kasa , so maintain ok?"

Nan ya dauko wata paper acikin wani file ya ajiye mata gaban desk dinta.

"Gashi na taimaka nabaki ba don halinki ba ko dan kinkai, sign and get lost"

Cize lips dinta nakasa tayi sannan ta dauki pen din hannunta nadan rawa, batareda ta karanta shirmen da'aka rubutaba tanemi inda zatasa hannu ta Dora hannu sama.

Shiru kamar bazatayiba saita daure tayi signing zuciyarta na wani irin karta.

Ajiye pen din tayi tana sauke ajiyar zuciya.

Shima dauka yayi yayi sign inda yakamata sannan yace
"DEAL!" Yana buga stamp akai.

Bata ankaraba taji ya fizgo hannunta na dama, saurin dagowa tayi tana kicin kicin kwace hannunta Amma takasa.

Wani box yafiddo a aljihunshi da hannu daya dayan na riqeda hannunta.

Budewa yayi sannan yafiddo wani hadadden zobe mai kyau yazuramata a yatsa ta karshe.

Kukane ya kufce mata zuciyarta kamar ana haura wuta.

"Welcome, welcome to the famous's world, ba suna kikeso ba zakiyi suna"

Yafada haryanzu yaqi sakin hannun.

Zaremata glass din idanunta yayi yana kallonta.

"Idan kika zare wannan ring din... Deal cancelled! Kuma kinsan har tsinemiki kwadayayyen babanki na iyayi"

Yayi wurgi da hannun a kyamace.

"Get lost, gobe by four zan aiko driver ya dauko ki ki kasance cikin shiri. GET LOST!"

Yafada yana komawa bisa kujerar shi.

Ahankali ta dago idanunta ta zubamashi, gabanshi ne yafadi ganin kallon tsantsan tsana datake mashi.

"Mekuma kike jira, ki 6acemin nace"

Glass dinta ta dauka Daga kan desk din still tana kallonshi sannan ahankali ta bude baki cikin wata iriyar murya tace

"I HATE YOU....WITH PASSION"

sannan tajuya tafice cikin sassarfa.

Bin kofar yake da kallo kamar still tananan, zuciyarshi namashi saqe saqe.


Unlike ranan yau ahankali tafito, ta maida glass dinta don haka babu Wanda yasan yanayin fuskarta.

Wuce Helen tayi ko kallonta batayi ba, itakau Helen tabita da kallon tuhuma.



Mota tashiga ta tada sannan ta figeta da wani irin gudu ta halba titi...✍

016





Tuqi take Amma ita kanta tasan kariyar Allah ce kawai ke tareda ita, Jitake kamar tacire zuciyarta ta jefar saboda radadi

'He blackmailed me'
'He made me beg'
'He forced me'

Wasu hawaye suka qara gangarowa fuskarta ta sharesu afusace.

Qara gudun motar tayi, batayi koina ba sai gidan maminta (inda take aure)


Budemata gate akayi ta Danna hancin motarta ciki.

A parking space tayi parking Saidai takasa fitowa, Duk Jitake jikinta kamar ba nataba , ga wani Sara da kanta keyi.


Tafi minti biyar ahakan sannan tasamu tafito dakyar hannu daya dafe da kai.

Kwankwasa kofar tayi sannan ta murda tashiga da sallama.

Babu kowa a falon kasancewar Duk qannenta ('ya'yan mamy) suna Maiduguri wajen kakansu Hutu.

Su biyar mamy ta Haifa a wannan gidan.

Aminulah dan shekara 16, sai kamalideen dan shekara 14, sai Ibrahim 11, habeeb 09 sai auta Abdul baseet 05.

Saudart nason qannenta sosai suma haka suna sonta sosai, Duk weekend idan tazo fira suke sha kamar me? Akwai shaquwa sosai tsakaninsu.


Zubewa tayi kan three seater din falon tana dafe kai.

Tafi mintuna biyar ahakan kafin mamynta tafito Daga kitchen da alama girki take.

Da farko bata lura daita ba saida tashigo falon sosai, tsoro taso bata data ga mutum kwance a falo.

Saida ta qaraso sannan tagane Saudart ce

"Saudart?"

Bude jajjayen idanunta dasukayi mata nauyi tayi ta kalleta saita tashi zaune a kasalance.

Qarasowa mamy tayi ta zauna itama daf da ita.

"Saudart lafiya?"

"Mamy ina wuni?"

"Lfy lau, meya sameki ne? Ji idanunki, ga muryar ki ma"

"Mamy bana jindadi ne" tafada tana kallon qasa.

"Kamar ya? Kallo daya za'a yimiki asan kinyi kuka, fadamin menene"

Girgiza kai tayi alamun babu komai.

"Wajen aikinkine?"

Nanma girgiza kai tayi

"Ko babanki ne?"

Murmushin takaici tayi sannan tace
"Mum please, nace babu komai, bana jindadi ne, kaina ke ciwo" tafada tana dafe kai.

"To Allah ya sauwaqe taso kishiga daki kisha magani ki kwanta.

Na musu ta tashi tabita wani daki, acan mamy ta bata magani sannan ta umarceta da ta kwanta tasamu barci.

Kasa barcin tayi koda mammyn tafita.

Qurawa ceiling kawai tayi tana tunane tunane.

Motsi kadan saita girgiza kai tana murmushin takaici.


Ahaka barci ya dauketa. Bata farkaba sai four shima mamy ta tadata tayi Sallah, da to kawai ta amsa dukda ba sallar takeba.

Watsa ruwa tayi a bandakin dakin sannan tafito.

Saida ta cika cikinta bam sannan ta bar gidan Bayan mamy tata bara shawarwari Masu amfani.

Gida tanufa kai tsaye, yanzu tarage jin zugin zuciyarta.

Horn daya tayi aka Budemata.

Da sallama tashiga falo ta hango dad zaune yana amsa waya

"Ok hang on zan kiraka" yafada yana tsinke wayar sannan ya miqe yanufota yana dariya.

Rungumeta yayi cikin jindadi yana ta suburbuda mata albarka don burinshi yacika, harma yaji alert.

Itadai Saudart iyakarta murmushi Wanda bana komai bane saina takaici.

Sai nan nan yake da ita, lokacin barci ma dakanshi yakaita daki yayi mata addu'a sannan yakashe mata wuta yajawo mata kofa.

Murmushin takaici tasakeyi tana girgiza kai.

Ta dade kafin barci Yaa dauketa, don data runtse ido abinda yafaru dazu take gani.

Dakyar tasamu barci ya dauketa can biyun dare.
Asuba tagari😴







Washegari bata wani damun kanta wajen shirin bakery ba, don bazata jeba, wanka kawai tayi ta kintsa kanta sannan tahau yin aiki a laptop.

Haryanzu fuskarta a cunkushe yake don haryanzu bata warwareba Daga abinda yafaru jiya.

Zobe kuwa bata cire shiba, yana a yatsarta ko meyasa oho?

Daddy ma yau be fitaba Wai zai tayata zaman gida tunda batajin dadi. 

Saidai waya dayake tayi da mutane akan business, kallo daya zaka mashi kasan yana cikin farinciki.

Hakan yasa itama Saudart taji Dama Dama don farincikin daddynta natane.



3:40

Suna zaune a falo, Saudart na kallo Alhaji na aiki a laptop sukaji qarar door bell.

Tashi tayi tana cewa "bari naduba"

Koda tabude maigadi tagani tsaye, fuska a washe suka gaisa tana tambayarshi lfy?

"Hajiya wani ne yazo daukanki"

"Wani?"

"Eh hajiya"

"Tofah wanene?"

Alhaji shamsu shima yataso

"Shalele menene?"

"Dad Wai wani yazo daukata Wai"

"Dauka? Waye?"

"Wlh Alhaji nima bansanshiba"

"Cemashi ya qaraso"


Sunanan tsaye saiga wani saurayi ya qaraso cikin shigar suit.

A ladabce ya gaida Alhaji, ya amsa itadai Saudart nata ido.

"Tofah, kaikuma Daga ina?"

"Sir, sir A.A yace nazo na dauko madam"

Kallon juna Saudart da Alhaji sukayi.
Sai asannan Saudart ta tuna dayace mata zai aiko driver qarfe hudu, ca6 aikau za'a yita.

"Shalele, dagaske ne?"

"Tayaya za'ayi insani daddy? Nima bansaniba, kai kaje ka sake tambaya qila 6atan hanya kayi"

Tafada tana komawa ciki.

Alhaji ya maido kallonshi kan saurayin "ka tabbata nan aka aikoka?"

"Eh Sir, nanne"

"Ok kajira ina zuwa"





Hmm yau ake yinta, don firr Saudart taqi yarda da buqatar daddy

"Dad ya kakeso danine? Ni matarshi ce dazai wani aiko azo a dauko ni? Gidan ubanwa ma zai kaini? Dad kaima kasan this is not proper"


"Saudart..."

"Daddy nayima biyyaya, bada son rainaba na amince da AUREN KWANGILA, ka tilastani nayima biyyaya, Dan Allah karka tilastamin wannan saboda ina gudun in bijirema"


"Saudart, wannan fa abin ba komai bane kawai..."

"Agarekane ba komai ba dad, agarekane ba komai ba, daddy ka daina sona, Baka sona, kafi son kudi akaina? Kafison dukiya akaina? Kafison farantama wani akaina?" Saikuma tafashe da kuka.

Sosai jikin daddy yayi Sanyi, rungumota yayi yafara rarrashinta cikin baiwarshi ta dadin baki.

Yasha wahala kafin yashawo Kanta ta yarda zataje.

Fita yayi yabata wuri don tashirya.

Yana fita ta Dora babin kukanta saida tayi mai isanta sannan tashige bayi tayi wanka.


Da gangan taita Jan jiki sai wajajen 4:30pm tagama shirin.

Izuwa yanzu Daga Alhajin har drivern sungaji dajira.

Ahankali ta sauko, yauma kamar jiya idanunta dode cikin NO RESPECT

Sakin baki daddy yayi ganin irin masifataccen kyan datayi.

Sanye take ciki Jan less mai touches din baqi, anmata style din Riga fitted da skirt mai wrapper, gashi ta cogale kallabin Kayan tayi daurin ture Kaga tsiya, sai baqin gyale a kafada yayinda ta lullu6a fuskarta da baqin shade.

Tayi kyau harta gaji dukda bawani kwalliya tayiba.

Fuskar nan a tamke, kana ganinta kasan bazata bar kota yiniba bare ta kwana.

Yau saita gwadama A.A ko mema ake kiranshi wacece Saudart, yanzu bayada dammar blackmailing dinta tunda yariga ya turama dad kudaden.

"Wow! Sweetheart you look soo takeaway!"

Dan ta6e baki tayi sannan tace thanks ahankali.

"To kuyi maza kutafi please Saudart behave"

Bata amsaba tafice taje tasamu driver Wanda harya gaji da ji ranta.

017






Cikin wani irin taku ta qarasa motar kafin tayi yunqurin budewa har driver din ya Budemata kofar baya aladabce harda dan russunawa.

Ta6e baki tayi sannan tashiga, rufewa yayi ya zagayo gaba yashiga.

Dad keta faman Daga mata hannu, yitayi kamar bata ganiba ahaka suka fice.

Ta6e baki Alhaji shamsu yayi, "kedai kika sani mutum arziqi na kiranshi yana guduwa"

Yaja tsaki yakoma ciki.




Shiru motar tayi, babu mai magana, tunda Saudart take bata ta6a shiga irin wannan motarba, watakau tahadu harta gaji, gashi kamar ba tafiya takeba don ko alamun tafiya bakaji.

Ga Sanyi mai hade da qamshi mai dadi Wanda ke saurin sa barci yakamaka idan Baka sababa.

Itama Saudart saida tayi dagaske don karta 6ingire, watakan idan kana cikin motar bakama sanin ana wani Abu waishi rana Awaje.

Haka taita kallon waje ta window hankali kwance, ganin ba hanyar A.A ENTERPRISES yabiba yasata muskutawa tace

"Mallam Wai ina zaka kaini ne haka?"

Cikin ladabi yace
"Kiyi haquri madam mun kusa zuwa"

Afusace tace "bashi na tambayekaba, where are you taking me to nace"

"Kiyi hqr madam mun kusa" yafada yana shan wata corner.

Masifa tashiga zazzaga mashi akan ya maidata inda ya daukota koya ajiyeta bata zuwa.

Shidai ko uffan beceba harta gaji tayi shiru.


A Gaban wani tangamemen gate ya tsaya yana horn.

Saida akayi scanning dinsu sannan gate din ya budu suka shiga.


Tun cikin motar tasaki baki tana kallon wajen.

Tunda take bata ta6a ganin qayattacen waje irin wannan ba, Waima ahakan tana cikine bata fitoba.

"Madam munzo, please come out" inji drivern da har yazagayo yabude mata.

Wani kallo ta watsa mashi Wanda bemasan tanayi ba saboda glass din daya kare idanunta.

"Are you serious? Nan inane ka kawoni?"

Kafin yasamu zarafin amsamata tajiyo muryar wani nacewa
"A'a? Harkun iso?"

Daga kai tayi ta kalleshi taga Ashe Wanda take ganine a office din A.A (sadeeq)

Cikin fara'a yadan qara Budemata murfin kofar yana cewa
"Bismillah gimbiya"

Cikin tsuke fuska tace "Wai inane nan? Kuma me nakeyi anan?"

"Yi hqr madam, wani dan shagalin nasarar da companynmu da kingin rassashi yasamu muka hada shine kema aka gayyaceki" yafada cikin fara'a.

Kamar tasake mgn saikuma tayi shiru.

"Please kiyi hqr kifito"

Kamar bazata fitoba sai can ta ziro kafarta a yangace tafito.

'Ya sallam!' Tayi exclaiming ganin zallar haduwa da wajen yayi.

Ga furranni ata koina.
Allah ya taimaketa akwai glass a idanunta da an lura da kauyancinta.

"Ma'am mu qarasa yana cikin waccan motar" inji sadeeq yana nuna wata dalleliyar mota fara qall 

Bin inda ya nunamata tayi da kallo sannan ta kauda kai.

"Please ma'am Ku kadai ake jira a hall din"

Cikin tsantseni tace "shi bazai iya fitowa bane, am going nowhere" ta maida Kallonta kan wayar hannunta tana shafawa.

'Lallai ahe wannan tafishi ma girman kai' yafada cikin zuciyarshi.

"Ok bari na kirashi" saiya juya yanufi inda motar take.


Ashraf Dama tundazu su yake kallo, ganin sadeeq yataho shi kadai yasa ranshi qara 6aci.

Dama gashi famm yake saboda latti dasukayi gashi yanzu tana botsarewa, lallai saiya koyamata hankali.

Kwankwasa glass din motar yasashi sakin siririn tsaki yana kauda kai.

Budewa Sadeeq yayi yana cewa "to saika fito gimbiya dai taqi Qarasowa"

Banza yayi dashi ko kallo be isheshi ba.

"Ashraf?"

Wani kallo ya watsa mashi yasake dauke kai.

"Please Wai bakusan kun tara mutane bane? Haba jira babu dadi"

Nan ma shiru.

"Wohoho Ashraf for goodness sake dakai fa Nike"

Harara ya watsa mishi yana cewa "cancel the gathering"

"Me?! Are you serious?!" Yafada cikin Waro idanu

Harara yasake watsa mishi "you heard me ai"

"Haba Ashraf? Ka gama tara mutane kayi wasting din time dinsu sai kuma ka soke taruwar, wannan wane irin wulaqanci ne"

"Look sadeeq karfa ka manta matsayinka, the fact that kai abokinane bazai Baka damar mayar dani shashasha ba, am still your boss!" Yafada tsakankannin haqora cikin Fushi.

"Kayi hqr Ashraf Amma..."

"Just shut up! Tagama 6atamin lokaci sannan tace bazata qarasoba? Ita wacece? Na ta6a jiran mace? Kai shaidane ban ta6aba sai akanta saikuma tanemi rainamin hankali? Cancel the damn party kazo mutafi!" 

Kallonshi kawai sadeeq keyi ganin dagaske fah yake nufin Ayi cancelling din partyn Bayan Duk manyan mutane aka tara, lallai aikau bazata sa6uba.

Kwantar dakai yayi yaita roqonshi harya yarda dakyar yafito.

Izuwa yanzu har biyar darabi tayi.

Saudart nacikin motar don bazata juri Tsayuwa ba, itama a 6angarenta aqule take, lallai wannan gayen dan wulaqanci ne, Dama sawa yayi akawota don ya shanyata.

Ta cikin motar ta hango fitowarshi, ta6e baki tayi tana kauda kai.

Sanye yake cikin farar suit qall, sai jar shirt dake ciki da Jan necktie irin dan qaraminnan, sai hanki ja daya dan leqo ta aljihun gaba.

Wow, gaskiya A.A haddadene👌 ba qaramin kyau shigar sukayi mashi ba.

Tare suka taho da Sadeeq dake Bayan Ashraf.

Suna isowa wajen dazasu bi su shiga ciki yaja ya tsaya hannaye zube cikin aljihu, fuska tamke ga shima uban baqin shade daya kwama.

Ganin haka yasa sadeeq qarasawa motar Saudart don tahowa da ita.

Saida tasake Jan aji sannan tafito itama sannan suka tako wajen Ashraf.

Shikau Sadeeq sai ayyana yadda dan zamansu zai kaya don ya lura dukansu yan jin Kaine.

Koda sukazo wajenshi ko gefenshi bata kallaba kamar yadda shima yayi kamar besan da itaba.

"Ina zuwa" inji Sadeeq yayi gaba don zuwa sanarda isowarsu.

Haka suka tsaya ko nuna alamun sunsan da zaman juna basuyiba.

Daga nesa idan ka hangesu saisun burgeka don dukkansu sun hadu ba karya ga kayansu daya kusan marching.
Ita jaa da baqi shi fari da jaa.


Yadda yabarsu haka ya tardasu.

"Please Ku qaraso"

Nanma rasa wanda zai fara takawa akayi

"Please Ku ake jira kuyi hqr" inji Sadeeq daya gaji da dramar su.

Nan Saudart taci girma tafara takawa sannan fa dan jinkan shima yatako.

"Please kubar tafiya aware kufa fiancée ne"

Babu Wanda ya tankamashi suka cigaba da tafiya.

Haka suka qarasa entrance din, DJ na hangosu ya saki wani kida mai dadi.

Take kallo yakoma kansu, kowa na yaba haduwarsu.

Tafi aka dauka hall din anatayi har suka qarasa wajen zamansu.

'Ashe surprise Sir A.A zaiyi Masu? Ashe da masoyiyarshi zaizo wannan party din' haka kowa yaita saqawa yayinda mafi yawan matan dake hall din Kishi ya cika musu zuciya.

Mutane sukayi tazura mazauninsu Bayan sun zauna suna tayasu Murnar nasarar d company dinsu yayi da kuma taya Murnar samun mata.

Sai a sannan Ashraf yayi danasanin daukota don shifa yayi hakanne don ya gwadamata koshi wanene dakuma yadda yakeda iko.

Hasken flashes din hotuna kawai ke haskemasu fuska. 
Ashraf kamar koda yaushe fuskarshi a tamke itakau Saudart babu yabo babu fallasa idan kuma akayi congratulating dinta sai tadan saki murmushi.

Ji take kamar ta tashi ta ruga don sosai tajita ta takura.

Dakyar akasamu mutane suka koma suka zazzauna.

Nan m.c yahau jawabin abinda ya tarasu cikin harshen turanci.

Itadai Saudart kawai tana wajen ne Amma hankalinta Duk yayi gida, Jitake wama yasa ta yarda Tun farko da zywan?

Duk inda ka wurga idanu yan media ne Masu dauka wannan mostly sunfi daukar su Ashraf.

Ashraf kau abinne yaso juyemashi don ba haka yasoba.

So yayi yakawota don ta raina kanta kuma beta6a tunanin yan jarida zasu hallarci wajen ba.

Kawai yakawotane don taga matsayinshi dakuma ikonshi.


Bayan jawaben nan aka shiga ci dasha, kowa da zaune a tebyr dinshi yana dan ta6a wani Abu.

Hakan take awajensu Ashraf. Dukda babu mai cin komai cikinsu, kowa da abinda yasha mishi kai.

Sadeeq ne yaqaraso wajen dawasu yan jarida biyu.

"Sir, gawasu yan media zasuyima kai da sarauniyarka tambayoyi" inji Sadeeq aladabce Saidai deep down dariya yake mishi.

Takaici ya hana Ashraf cewa komai don sai yanzu yasan Sadeeq ne ya gayyato mashi yan jaridar nan.

"Sir wane irin farinciki kake ciki ayau?" Inji wani yana saita mic dinshi gabanshi

Shiru yayi kamar bazeyi mgnba saiya daure cikin muryarshi mai dadin amo yace
"Ina cikin farinciki sosai"

"Sir wannan ne karo na farko da akafara ganinka da mace, ko zaka iya gayamana matsayinta agareka?"

Inji wani nakusada nafarkon.

Nanma shiru,

"Lallai Sadeeq you are in hot soup" yafada cikin zuciyarshi

Can cikin murya qasa qasa yace
"She's my fiancée"

"Wow congratulations... Ma'am zaki iya fadamana farincikin dakike ciki?"

Suka maida akalar tambayar wajen Saudart.

Jimm tadanyi sannan itama ayangace tace
"Ina cikin farinciki sosai"

"Ma'am wani matsayine sir A.A ke dashi awajenki"

Murmushi tadan saki

"Kamar yadda yafada am he's fiancée"

"Wow.. Zaki iya fadamana farkon haduwarku?"

Woo! Nabani, tafada cikin zuciyarta

"Eh"

"Ok muna jinki ma'am"

"Mun fara haduwane a bakery dina" tafada kai tsaye

"Wane bakery kenan?" Inji dayan.

"Alhairi bakery"

"Omg, badai kece mai alhairi bread ba?" Inji dayan cikin mammaki.

"Yes nice" ta amsa cikin basarwa.

Ashraf na gefe takaici kamar yayi hauka.


"Me sir A.A yajeyi a bakeryn?"

Murmushin gefen baki tayi irin Wanda shima yakeyi.

"Me zaije yi kau? Yaje Isar da saqon zuciyarshi ne"

"Wow! Me hakan ke nufi?" Inji dayan sai setasu da camera ake.

Dukda tagaji da tambayoyin Amma burinta na quntatawa Ashraf yasa tace
"Ina nufin yazone donyayi fighting for his love"

"Wow amazing! Sir Ashraf hakane?" Inji dayan yana saita Ashraf da mic.

Jiyayi kamar ya nutse don kunya don Dama tunda suka fara hankalin kowa yadawo Kansu.

Babu damar musawa yayi murmushi yana kada kai.

"Sir idan hakane akwai inda kafara ganinta kenan harka fola Mata, inane kafara ganinta?"

Ca6, da ace ana ganin zuciya da kunga yadda zuciyar Ashraf ke tafarfasa.

"A cinema" yafada ahankali, dukda cikin Fushi yake hakan be nunaba a fuskarshi. Lallai wlh saita gane kurenta, shi take zubarma girma agaban jama'a? Wai har binta bakery ko ubanmi ma yayi?

"Wow gaskiya labarin haduwarku yayi dadi, ma'am da Sir A.A yazo wajenki da qoqon bararshi ya kikaji?"

Kutt.. Qoqon me? Inji Ashraf cikin zuciya.

Cikin basarwa Saudart tace "well as expected nayi mammakin hakan, ganin yanayin halinmu ba dayaba. At first naqi yarda da soyayyarshi gaskiya ce Amma ganin yadda yaketa zarya bakery dina Dama gidanmu yasani giving abun a second thought, ahankali ahankali nafara kulashi har yayi nasarar yaqar zuciyata da soyayyarshi" tafada murmushin mugunta fall fuskarta


Wohoho nan hall din ya rude da hayaniya kowa na fadin albarkacin bakinshi, Shidai Ashraf komawa yayi yayi balancing akan kujerar tareda lumshe idanu, zuciyarshi kamar ana hura wuta.

dakyar hall din yayi shiru sannan daya Daga cikin yan jardan yace "yanzu zaki iya fadamana wane matsayin yake dashi azuciyarki?" 

Murmushi tadan saki a kunyace sannan tace
"Yanada babban matsayi azuciyata sbd mutum neshi mai iya tarairaya, iya tarairayarshi da kulawarshi yasani fara sonshi, gaskiya am lucky to have such a caring guy"

Caraf dan jaridan yayi yace "shima he is lucky wajen samun kyakyawar sarauniya irinki, kou Mr A.A?"

Bude idanunshi yayi tacikin glass wadda ba'a ma hango idanun. A hankali yace
"Yeah...am indeed.. Lucky"

Tafi aka dauka gabadaya hall din, sai haskesu da flashes ake, wasu dan iyayi har zuwa wajensu suke sudau selfie.

Wasu yan rawar kan kau sai liqema Saudart suke ala dole zasu qulla abota da masoyiyar the famous billionaire A.A

Itakau Saudart ko ajikinta, ko babu komai ta rama koda kadanne cikin wulaqancin da Ashraf yayi Mata don haka jinta take wasai.

Oga kau a zahiri kawai yake garas Amma karka tona zuciyarshi, jiyake kamar ya tashi yabar hall din, Allah Allah yake agama damn gathering din...✍


Ummin fasihu ce🧚‍♀

(Contract marriage)

Allah ka ji6anci lamuranmu, karka barmu da kanmu🤲



Wannan page din nakine ummin bilal da Duk members din AUREN KWANGILA NOVEL GROUP Amma fa banda yan le6el😏


Ngd da addu'o'inku agareni🙏
Allah yabar zumunci🤲



Story written by Ashaanty love
(Ummin fasihu)




017






Cikin wani irin taku ta qarasa motar kafin tayi yunqurin budewa har driver din ya Budemata kofar baya aladabce harda dan russunawa.

Ta6e baki tayi sannan tashiga, rufewa yayi ya zagayo gaba yashiga.

Dad keta faman Daga mata hannu, yitayi kamar bata ganiba ahaka suka fice.

Ta6e baki Alhaji shamsu yayi, "kedai kika sani mutum arziqi na kiranshi yana guduwa"

Yaja tsaki yakoma ciki.




Shiru motar tayi, babu mai magana, tunda Saudart take bata ta6a shiga irin wannan motarba, watakau tahadu harta gaji, gashi kamar ba tafiya takeba don ko alamun tafiya bakaji.

Ga Sanyi mai hade da qamshi mai dadi Wanda ke saurin sa barci yakamaka idan Baka sababa.

Itama Saudart saida tayi dagaske don karta 6ingire, watakan idan kana cikin motar bakama sanin ana wani Abu waishi rana Awaje.

Haka taita kallon waje ta window hankali kwance, ganin ba hanyar A.A ENTERPRISES yabiba yasata muskutawa tace

"Mallam Wai ina zaka kaini ne haka?"

Cikin ladabi yace
"Kiyi haquri madam mun kusa zuwa"

Afusace tace "bashi na tambayekaba, where are you taking me to nace"

"Kiyi hqr madam mun kusa" yafada yana shan wata corner.

Masifa tashiga zazzaga mashi akan ya maidata inda ya daukota koya ajiyeta bata zuwa.

Shidai ko uffan beceba harta gaji tayi shiru.


A Gaban wani tangamemen gate ya tsaya yana horn.

Saida akayi scanning dinsu sannan gate din ya budu suka shiga.


Tun cikin motar tasaki baki tana kallon wajen.

Tunda take bata ta6a ganin qayattacen waje irin wannan ba, Waima ahakan tana cikine bata fitoba.

"Madam munzo, please come out" inji drivern da har yazagayo yabude mata.

Wani kallo ta watsa mashi Wanda bemasan tanayi ba saboda glass din daya kare idanunta.

"Are you serious? Nan inane ka kawoni?"

Kafin yasamu zarafin amsamata tajiyo muryar wani nacewa
"A'a? Harkun iso?"

Daga kai tayi ta kalleshi taga Ashe Wanda take ganine a office din A.A (sadeeq)

Cikin fara'a yadan qara Budemata murfin kofar yana cewa
"Bismillah gimbiya"

Cikin tsuke fuska tace "Wai inane nan? Kuma me nakeyi anan?"

"Yi hqr madam, wani dan shagalin nasarar da companynmu da kingin rassashi yasamu muka hada shine kema aka gayyaceki" yafada cikin fara'a.

Kamar tasake mgn saikuma tayi shiru.

"Please kiyi hqr kifito"

Kamar bazata fitoba sai can ta ziro kafarta a yangace tafito.

'Ya sallam!' Tayi exclaiming ganin zallar haduwa da wajen yayi.

Ga furranni ata koina.
Allah ya taimaketa akwai glass a idanunta da an lura da kauyancinta.

"Ma'am mu qarasa yana cikin waccan motar" inji sadeeq yana nuna wata dalleliyar mota fara qall 

Bin inda ya nunamata tayi da kallo sannan ta kauda kai.

"Please ma'am Ku kadai ake jira a hall din"

Cikin tsantseni tace "shi bazai iya fitowa bane, am going nowhere" ta maida Kallonta kan wayar hannunta tana shafawa.

'Lallai ahe wannan tafishi ma girman kai' yafada cikin zuciyarshi.

"Ok bari na kirashi" saiya juya yanufi inda motar take.


Ashraf Dama tundazu su yake kallo, ganin sadeeq yataho shi kadai yasa ranshi qara 6aci.

Dama gashi famm yake saboda latti dasukayi gashi yanzu tana botsarewa, lallai saiya koyamata hankali.

Kwankwasa glass din motar yasashi sakin siririn tsaki yana kauda kai.

Budewa Sadeeq yayi yana cewa "to saika fito gimbiya dai taqi Qarasowa"

Banza yayi dashi ko kallo be isheshi ba.

"Ashraf?"

Wani kallo ya watsa mashi yasake dauke kai.

"Please Wai bakusan kun tara mutane bane? Haba jira babu dadi"

Nan ma shiru.

"Wohoho Ashraf for goodness sake dakai fa Nike"

Harara ya watsa mishi yana cewa "cancel the gathering"

"Me?! Are you serious?!" Yafada cikin Waro idanu

Harara yasake watsa mishi "you heard me ai"

"Haba Ashraf? Ka gama tara mutane kayi wasting din time dinsu sai kuma ka soke taruwar, wannan wane irin wulaqanci ne"

"Look sadeeq karfa ka manta matsayinka, the fact that kai abokinane bazai Baka damar mayar dani shashasha ba, am still your boss!" Yafada tsakankannin haqora cikin Fushi.

"Kayi hqr Ashraf Amma..."

"Just shut up! Tagama 6atamin lokaci sannan tace bazata qarasoba? Ita wacece? Na ta6a jiran mace? Kai shaidane ban ta6aba sai akanta saikuma tanemi rainamin hankali? Cancel the damn party kazo mutafi!" 

Kallonshi kawai sadeeq keyi ganin dagaske fah yake nufin Ayi cancelling din partyn Bayan Duk manyan mutane aka tara, lallai aikau bazata sa6uba.

Wayarta taciro takira daddy taita mashi kuka.

Tananan kwance su baby suka shigo dakin, kamar hadin baki suka fada Mata ajiki.

Nanfa suka shiga tsokanarta baby na kareta, itadai Saudart banza tayi dasu don ba Sune gabanta ba.

Sai Daga baya baby tazame dankwalin Saudart taga kitson.

Nanma rudewa tayi don yau tamafi jiya rudewa.

Shikku akayi mata qananu an tamkesu da qaton ribbon ya sauko har wuya.

Nanma Wai hoton kitson zata dauka, dakyar ta hqr da daukar hoton don Saudart qin yarda tayi, su Nafeesa mezasuyi musu inba dariya ba suna musu ihun sunji Kansu.


Yauma sai kusan dayan dare suka kwanta, yayinda Saudart bata samu barci ba sai wajajen uku sbd yadda Taita juyi tana tunane tunane...✍

Nanfa aka dasa fira, uwar kaudi kau har gwada Masu irin rawar dazatayi take, kuma ba laifi ta iya rawa don sosai rawar tayimata kyau.

Haka sukaita hirarsu itadai Saudart na kwance tana jinsu idanu a lumshe, don abinda ya dameta ya daketa bata tasu takeba.

Nanfa suka kama aiki.

Ogan ita kema Amarya, yaran aikin kuma nama su yanmatan amaren.

Sai wajajen azahar aka gama.

Sosai qunshi ya hau da farar fatarta, suma su baby ba laifi nasu ma yayi kyau Saidai fa kunsan komai na Amarya yafi kyau.

Tafe suke da manya manyan robobi shake da snacks kama Daga cup cake, meat pie, doughnut, sausage roll, samosa, pizza, da dai sauransu.

Dayake harabar Nada girma sosai anan aka jera kujeru kowa ya zazzauna suna facing din inda mallamar ke zaune, itakau Saudart an tanadar mata mazaunin ta Daga gefen dama.

Saida komai ya lafa sannan aka fito da Amarya.

Wohoho nanfa kallo yakoma sama😳

Sanye take da atamfa Riga da skirt pieces Masu kalar jaa da fari saita Dora qatuwar alkyabba irinta ya'yan sarakuna fara qall mai aikin golden da zaiba , ta sanya hular alkyabbar wanda tarufe Rabin fuskarta.

Anan na hango su tawagar yan AUREN KWANGILA NOVEL GROUP sun Kasa zaune sun Kasa tsaye kowacce burinta tasamu rabonta.

Can gefe naga maman fateema da ummu arifullah suna leqa ledar juna don ganin me suka samu.

RANA BATA QARYA......

Yau ranar jumu'a ce mai cike da tarihi a rayuwar wasu, jumu'ar da bazasu ta6a mantawaba.

Yau ne ranar daurin aurensu, AUREN KWANGILA.

Tunda ta farka ko matsawa Daga inda take batayiba, dama ba Sallah takeba bare ta tashi tayi.

Tana kwance ido lumshe kamar mai barci Saidai idanunta biyu tana sauraron Duk wani zirga zirga da hayaniyar mutane.

*yau ne* tafada cikin zuciyarta

*yau ba gobeba* 
*yau zan zama matar aure*
*matar auren kwangila*
*matar mutumin da banajin ko digon sonshi daidai da qwayar zarra acikin zuciyata*
*matar aurenda nan da wani d'an lokaci zata zama baza wara*
*me kika yima kanki Saudart?*
*anya baki cuci kanki ba*
*anya daddy beso kanshi dayawa ba*
*inama ace mafarki ne*
*Allah yasa mafarki ne*
*Allah yasa ba gaske bane*

Hawaye suka silalo mata dukda idanun a rufe yake.

Wani nauyi taji zuciyarta nayi mata kamar an doramata qaton nutse a qirji.

Sosai hawayen keta silalowa batareda tayi wani yunqurin taresu ko sharesu ba.

Daidai nan mardeeya tashigo dama sunje amso dinkin anko dinsu ne dawowarsu kenan tabaro su baby qasa.

"Subhanalillah" tafada tana Qarasowa wajenta.

"Saudart" tafada tana dan jijjigata ganin idanunta haryanzu a rufe yake.

Banza tayi da ita Saidai hakan besa hawayen sun tsayaba.

"Sister menene? Dan Allah ki tashi, Meya faru?"

Nanma shiru saima juyamata baya datayi.

"Saudart kiyi hqr, nasan kukanki baya rasa nasaba da auren daza'a daura miki yau, Duk macen datasan ciwon kanta dole ta koka ranar aurenta ba don zata bar iyayenta kadaiba, don itama zata taka wani matsayi wanda bata ta6a takawaba a rayuwarta, nauye nauye zasu hau kanta wanda idan ba me dakkakiyar zuciya bace bazata iya dauke nauyin ba"

Kamo hannayenta tayi tariqe sannan cikin sigar rarrashi tace
"Sis kiyi hqr, Allah baya dorawa bawa abinda baya iyawa, ki kasance mai Neman tallafi a wajen Allah kuma ki kasance mai hqr, idan kinadashi ada ki Dora akai, darajar 'ya mace ke har namiji ma shine aure, ki kasance jajirttaciyar mace abun kwatance a fannin aure, ki zama abun alfahari ga mamy da daddy ke harma garemu gabaki daya, dukda aure rai gareshi idan ba'a mutu dashiba yakan mutu yabar ma'auratan don Allah aurenki yazama abin kwatance a family dinmu, babu yaji bare saki please, nafi kowa sanin yadda mamy ta kwallafa rai akan aurenki don sau ba adadi ina jinsu idan suna fira da ummina akan tanason kar aurenki yazama irin nata, tafison kiyi auren mutu-ka-raba, ya kasance yayanki duka nawajenki yadda zaki basu tarbiyya kuma su taso tare, please sister kicikama mamy wannan buri nata, ki jajirce sis, aure yanada dadi haka wani shafin idan aka bude yafi mad'aci daci, ki riqe Allah da manzonsa kuma ki riqe hqr.."

Shiru tayi ganin yadda kukan nata ya tsananta, shiru tayi tana kallon yadda take kukan, abinka ga ruwa ruwa sai itama taji digg digg hawaye sunfara digomata.

Nan aka rasa mai rarrashin wani cikinsu don hade kai wuri guda sukayi hannunsu cikin na juna sunata rizgar kuka.

Ita kukan Saudart ya Kasu kashi kashi, ga na fargabar aure da na barin iyaye gana fargabar yadda mamy zataji idan auren ya mutu.
Itakau mardeeya kukan tsantsar tausayinta take dama na mata gabadaya, wanda Daga inda kayi aure nauyi yahau kanka, gana miji, idan kuma aka hayyayafa gana 'ya'ya.

Ahaka su baby suka taddasu.

Turus sukayi abakin kofa suna kallonsu kowacce takasa motsi.

Baby ce ta fara takawa ta qarasa wajensu itama ta zauna ta rungumosu gabadaya itama ta bude nata muryar da Allah yabata tafara raira nata kukan.

Ganin hakan yasa itama Nafeesa tayi wajensu dagudu itama ta rungumosu sukaita kukan tare da wannan ya dauka sai wannan ya aje, da wannan ya aje sai wannan ya dauka.

(Nima ganin haka yasa nadan kauda kaina na matso guntun hawaye na😢 sannan na share da hanki)

Suna haka matar kawu bala tashigo, tana ganin yadda suka cure waje daya tafara sallalami tana tafa hannaye.

"Ni asiya mezan gani?"

Hakan yasasu dagowa Kowanne fuska jaga jaga da hawaye.

"Wannan wane irin sabon sakarcine zakuzo Ku cure waje daya kuna kuka? Meya faru?"

Nafeesa ta nunasu cikin muryar kuka tace "haka nisa baby mukazo muka tardasu suna kuka"

"Haka nazo na isketa nima tanayi"

"Na rarrasheta taqi shiru"

"Mtcheew ni matsamin dalla"

Tafada tana miqar daita tsaye suka nufi hanyar waje.

Sun kusan mintuna goma zaune jigum jigum babu mai magana.

2:30pm daidai aka daura auren ASHRAF AUWAL da SAUDATU SHAMSU KANKIYA.

031




Garin yayi tsit, yayi duhu saboda Daren yafara nisa, ga hadarin daya hadu Wanda yaqarawa Daren duhu, iska mai dadi sai qadawa yake.


Tuqi yake cikin normal speed yana sarrafa steering din gwanin burgewa.

Tsit motar kamar babu kowa aciki, kowanne da abinda yasha mishi kai babu Wanda yanuna yasan da wanzuwar Dan uwanshi.

Idanunshi da hankalinshi na kan kwalta ko gefenta yayinda itakuma take gefenshi lafe a kujera idanunta a lumshe.

Har yanzu takasa yarda wai ita Matar aurece, wata biyu dasuka wuce idan da wani zai gayamata warhaka tanada aure babu abinda zai hanata qaryatawa, amma sai gashi cikin Dan qanqanin lokaci labarin rayuwarta ya canza, acikin wata biyu tasamu miji har anyi auren saidai ba irin auren da aka saba yiba, aure ne na takaitaccen lokaci Wanda ke shimfide akan sharrud'a da tsari.

Ajiyar zuciya ta suke ahankali daidai Wanda taji ya dakatar da mortar yana horn.

Can kuma taji motar tacigaba da tafiya duk abinda ake idanunta na alumshe kuma batada niyyar budesu.


Direct parking space yanufa inda yake kwal babu mota ko daya kasancewar sabon gidane yau akafara amfani dashi.

Parking yayi sannan yakashe motar yakoma ya jingina da bayan kujerarshi yana lumshe hazal eyes dinshi.

Shiru motar ta dauka babu mai ko motsi, izuwa yanzu hadarin ya hadu sosai don iskar yaqara qarfi, sai walqiya da cida ake.

Hannu yasa cikin sanyi ya balle seat belt ya bude murfin motar batareda yako kalli gefentaba ya fita ya maida kofar yarufe, sannan yafara takawa cikin takunshi na qasaita yawuce.


Ajiyar zuciya ta sauke nannauya, ahankali ta bude idanunta Wanda tunda suka baro wajen dinner suke a lumshe.

Tacikin mirror din gefen motar tabishi da kallo harya shige ciki.

Ta6e baki tayi cikin takaici, ita tunda take bata ta6a ji ko ganin ango yabar amaryarshi amota ba ranar auren su.

Koda yake auren ma gabadaya bata ta6a jin irin nasuba don haka duk abinda yabiyo bayama ba komai bane.


Hannu tasa ta bude kofar itama sannan ta ziro kafaffunta ta sauko.

Qanqame jikinta tayi a tsorace jin anyi wata irin tsawa da walqiya, saurin maida kofar tayi tarufe tana qanqame net din data Dora akai Wanda iska ke baraxanar fecewa dashi.

Ahankali ta fara takawa itama tanufi hanyar dataga yabi hannu daya dafe da net din kanta dayan kuma ya tattaro qasan gown dinta dake sharar qasa.


Dakyar tasamu ta isa main door sbd wuyar tafiya da heels din kafarta kesata.

Hannu tasa a handle din kofar ta murda saigashi yabude, tura kofar tayi tashiga bakinta dauke da addu'o'i.

Wani sanyi da ni'imtaccen qamshi yaimata maraba Wanda saida ta lumshe ido don dadi.

Bin qayyatacen falon tayi da idanu tana jinjina 6arnar kudin da Dad yayi wajen zubamata kayan daki na gani na fada.

*Lallai dad* tafada acikin zuciyarta.

Haka taita bin falon da kallo tanata yan ta6e ta6en baki.

Jin tsayuwar ya isheta gakuma nauyin kayan jikinta yasata fara takawa tanufi matattakalar benen datagani daga gefen dama.

Ahankali taita taka mattatakalar harta kai sama.

Dakuna uku ke saman ajere.

Tsayawa tayi tana kallonsu tana tunanin wane ne nata.

Tsaki taja cikin takaici, wai ace Amarya ke Neman dakinta, kai gaskiya dad ya cuceta, kwata kwata ba haka ta tsara aurentaba, ta Dade tana qiyasta yadda rayuwar auren ta zai kasance, ta jima tana qiyasta yadda auren ta zai zama abun koyi da burgewa ga mutane da dama, amma rana daya an rusamata tsari.

Jitayi ankece da ruwan sama kamar dabakin qwarya.

Ajiyar zuciya ta sauke sannan tanufi dakin farko, tana murdawa taji gamm.

Tsaki tasake ja ta nufi ta tsakiyar, tana murdawa taji tabude.

Tsayawa tayi tana kokwanton shiga don bata fatan ganin fuskarshi nan kusa.

Fasa shiga tayi tanufi ta ukun ta murda taji itama gamm hakan yasata dawowa ta tsakiyar badon tasoba.

Tura kofar tayi ahankali sannan tashiga a darare.

Saida ta leqa koina ta tabbatarda babu kowa aciki sannan hankalinta yakwanta.

Ta Dade zaune tana kwararo addu'o'i sannan ta shafa tamike ta cire hijabin tanufi gadon don bacci ke idanunta sosai.

Dama ita masoyiyar damina ce, tana bala'in son ruwan sama musanmman na dare, tana jindadin yin barci ana ruwan sama.

Bata wani Dade akwanceba wani nauyayyen barci mai dadi yayi gaba daita.

A bangaren ango kau dama yana shiga yacire babbar rigar don ba qaramin takuramashi tayiba.

Direct toilet yashige don wanka.

Koda yafi to kayan barci kawai yasa ya hada coffee da coffee maker dake dakin ya zauna yana kur6a hankali kwance kamar be baro diyar mutaneba awaje.

Yana cikin sha aka kece da ruwan sama sai a sannan tunaninta yafado mashi.

Ta6e baki yayi yacigaba dashan coffee dinshi har yashanye.

Yana gama yashige cikin bargo shima ya kwanta don shima yana son ruwan dare sosai.

Shima be jimaba barci ya daukeshi

032



Kiraye kirayen sallar asuba ya tadata, bude idanunta daketa faman rufewa dakansu tayi tana hamma da alamu dai barcin be ishetaba.

Tashi tayi zaune tana miqa tana salati

033





Washegari ma bata fitoba saida ta tabbatar da yabar gidan, sannan tafito ta samarma kanta abinda zataci ta gyara gidan ta goge Tass ta saka turaren wuta sannan tayi hayewarta sama.

Ba ita ta saukoba sai bayan azahar ta nufi kitchen ta Dora abinda zata sakama cikinta sannan ta gyare kitchen din ta tattara abincin tayi sama.

Yauma sai wajajen qarfe Tara ya dawo gidan, kamar jiya beko ni takan dakintaba yayi shigewarshi dakin shi.



Ataqaice dai haka sukaita wasan 6uya tsakaninsu, koko ince take wasan 6uya dashi don izuwa yanzu ta laqaici lokacin fitarshi da dawowarshi don haka ta rage zaman sama, tana saukowa qasa ta yini amma da tayi sallar isha'i kuma ita da saukowa sai Allah ya kaimu kuma.


Tanada kwana biyar su mardeeya su kazo harda baby don biyamusu tayi su kazo tare.

Ranar kau saudart taga ta kanta don tisata gaba sukayi da tsokana iri iri.

Tun tana maida martani harta haqura, ita kau baby wani sa'in ta shigarmata wani sa'in ta koma masu Nafeesa su tararmata.

Basu suka bar gidanba sai qarfe shidda da Rabi na marece bayan ta cikasu da kyauta na kayan kwalliya da snacks ta rakosu har wajenda motar baby take don aciki su kazo.

Jitake kamar tabisu don zaman kadaicin ya isheta gashi tayi missing din daddynta sosai dukda kullum cikin waya suke.

Ahaka sukayi bankwana cikin mararin juna saudart na musu addu'ar Allah ya tsare kasancewar su mardeeya gobe zasu koma Maiduguri.

Ba ita takoma cikiba saida taga fitarsu.

Bin harabar gidan tayi da kallo don yau ne karon farko data fito harabar tun zuwanta.

Bin wajen taitayi da kallo don ya qayatu iya qayatuwa ga trimmed flowers daya zagaye wajen gwanin burgewa.

Ta6e bakinta tayi ta jiya ta koma ciki don har anfara kiraye kirayen sallar magrib.

Yauma kamar kullum tana bata sake saukowa ba bayan isha'i.


Kwanci tashi yau kwananta sha bakwai a gidan.

A yanayin zamantakewarsu babu wani chanji don rabonda Susa juna a idanu tun ranar auren su.

Izuwa yanzu saudart tasake da gidan sosai babu inda bata saniba agidan.

Akwai komai agidan kama daga abinci da kayan more rayuwa.

Saidai tana cikin kadaici sosai, kullum ita kadai ke yini inba Allah yajefo mata wani baqoba, wani sa'in don debe kewa saita shiga garden dake bayan gidan don hutawa ko ta zauna falo tayi kallo.

Bakery dinta kau kullum tana samun bayanai akan yadda yake tafiya kuma alhamdullilah sai bunqasa yake.

Haka zalika kusan kullum sai sunyi waya da Ummy don izuwa yanzu tana Sakin jiki daita su danyi fira kasancewar Ummy batada matsala kuma tana sonta sosai don saudart badai hankali da nutsuwaba.

Wani sa'in idan kadaici ya isheta saita bugama Ummy ta roqeta akan baby tazo.

Duk zuwan da baby keyi bata yarda takai magrib take juyawa, saudart tasha yimata tayin kwana amma firr take qiyawa wai in taganta lahira kaita akayi.


A bangaren ashraf kuwa tuni yakoma bakin aikinsa, dama hutun sati daya ya dauka, shima saboda matsawar sadeeq.


Shi harga Allah wani sa'in mancewa yake da yanada mata, rabonda yasata a idanu tun awajen dinner.

Yasan haqqinshine yasan yaya take ciki dakuma kula da lafiyarshi amma bejin yana iya zuwa ganinta, aganinshi ai ba normal aure bane auren su, auren kwangila ne kowa da dalilinshi nayin auren kuma kowa da abinda yake targeting.






Jera abinci take bisa dining tanayi tana kada kai tana humming tana bin waqar datakeji ta earphones din kunnenta.

Saida ta shirya komai a table din sannan tayi sama tana Dan hadawa da tsalle tsalle Wanda duk acikin shauqin waqar datake jine.

Tana shiga tacire earphones din kunnenta ta fara tu6ewa don watsawa don yau garin badai zafiba, yadda akayi rana yau dakyar idan ba ruwan sama za'ayi ba. Tana gama ty6ewa ta dauki towel ta daura tashige toilet.



Horn yayi sau daya, nan aka shiga scanning din motar, bayan angama gate din ya wangale dakanshi ya kutsa kai yashiga.

A parking space yayi parking sannan yafito ya rufe kofar yayi locking din motar sannan yanufi cikin gida yana sassauta daurin necktie dinshi.

Murda handle din kofar yayi yashiga da sallama, kamar kullum, yauma wannan sanyayyar qamshin da harya fara kama dakin yayi mashi maraba.

Shaqa numfashi yayi ahankali sannan ya fesar, yau qamshin na dabanne don bayan na Wanda dakin yasabayi akwai wani kuma daban Wanda yakasa tantancewa.

Stairs yanufa cikin takunshi na qasaita yana hawa daya bayan daya harya isa sama.

Yauma kamar kodayaushe ko kallon saitin kofar beyiba ya bude kofar shi yashige.

Kasancewar tana toilet tafara wanka duk bataji shigowarshi ba, hasalima tasan lokacin dawowarshi don haka bata kawoma ranta dawowarshi yanzu ba.

Bayan yan mintuna tafito jikinta na digar ruwa, wucewa tayi closet direct don ga yadda ake zafinnan batajin zata iya shafama jikinta komai.

Budewa tayi ta tsaya hannaye riqeda kugu tana bin kayanta dake Jere gwanin kyau da kallo tana shawarar wanne yakamata tasaka.

Ta Dade tana ruwan ido kafin taciro wani three quarter din wando gari mai adon pink din zare a gefe gefen wandon sai mahadinshi wato armless pink vest mai zanen yar Tamar Barbie agaba sannan ta Parke gashinta tsakar kai tayi doughnut dashi sannan tasa wata farar hula marar nauyi.

Turare kawai ta fesa sannan tazura wasu pink baby shoes ta maida earphones dinta ta dauki wayarta tafita.

Harta zauna zata fara serving kanta taji tana sha'awar local lemu, tunawa tayi da lemun tamarin datagani dazu a group, ganin beda wuyar yi yasata tashi tashiga kitchen din don hadoshi.



Tana shiga yafito daga dakin cikin shigar qananun kaya ba Adidas.

Hannunshi daya cikin aljihu dayan kuma riqeda wayar dake kareda kunnenshi alamun waya yake.

A daya daga cikin qayyatatun kujerun falon ya zauna yayi irin balancing dinnan kamar wani Dan sarki ya Dora hannunshi dake cikin aljihu bisa kan kujerar yana cigaba da amsa wayar.


Cikin takunta tafito, hannunta daya riqeda wani haddaden jug, dayan kuma riqeda Glass cup.

Dining tanufa batareda takawoma ranta komai ba.

Serving din kanta tayi cikin plate sannan ta zuba drink din a glass cup tasaka straw aciki sannan ta zauna ta dauki spoon and fork tafara cin abincin cikin nutsuwa.


Tun fitowarta ya bar gane abinda ke wakana a wayar dasuke, da ido yabita tunda tafito har ta isa dining din.

Da farko kasa ganeta yayi, saida ta zauna tana facing dinshi sannan ya wayeta.


Kasa dauke idanu yayi akanta, duk wani motsi nata akan idanunshi, yadda kukasan anhada magnet tsakanin idanunshi da jikinta don kallonta yake bako kyaftawa.

Ita kau a bangarenta batamasan yanayiba don kwata kwata bata kawowa ranta da wani agidan bayan itaba, dukda tana jin alamun idanu akan ta amma bata maida hankali akaiba.


Ringing din wayarta yasata ajiye glass cup din datake tsotsar drink din ta dauki wayar tana duba mai kiran.

Ganin daddy ke kiran yasata katse kiran tana murmushi sannan tasake Kira.

Ta kara a kunne fuskarta fall murmushi sannan ta dauki cup din takai baki tana kur6a.

Kamar ance ta dago, sai caraf idanunshi suka hade.

Wani wawan zuwa tayiwa lemun abinka da tsamiya nan take tahaumata bisa kai tafara tari cikin fitar hayyaci Wanda har tana saukowa qasa...✍

Tun tana maida martani harta haqura, ita kau baby wani sa'in ta shigarmata wani sa'in ta koma masu Nafeesa su tararmata.

Basu suka bar gidanba sai qarfe shidda da Rabi na marece bayan ta cikasu da kyauta na kayan kwalliya da snacks ta rakosu har wajenda motar baby take don aciki su kazo.

Jitake kamar tabisu don zaman kadaicin ya isheta gashi tayi missing din daddynta sosai dukda kullum cikin waya suke.

Ahaka sukayi bankwana cikin mararin juna saudart na musu addu'ar Allah ya tsare kasancewar su mardeeya gobe zasu koma Maiduguri.

Ba ita takoma cikiba saida taga fitarsu.

Bin harabar gidan tayi da kallo don yau ne karon farko data fito harabar tun zuwanta.

Bin wajen taitayi da kallo don ya qayatu iya qayatuwa ga trimmed flowers daya zagaye wajen gwanin burgewa.

Ta6e bakinta tayi ta jiya ta koma ciki don har anfara kiraye kirayen sallar magrib.

Yauma kamar kullum tana bata sake saukowa ba bayan isha'i.


Kwanci tashi yau kwananta sha bakwai a gidan.

A yanayin zamantakewarsu babu wani chanji don rabonda Susa juna a idanu tun ranar auren su.

Izuwa yanzu saudart tasake da gidan sosai babu inda bata saniba agidan.

Akwai komai agidan kama daga abinci da kayan more rayuwa.

Saidai tana cikin kadaici sosai, kullum ita kadai ke yini inba Allah yajefo mata wani baqoba, wani sa'in don debe kewa saita shiga garden dake bayan gidan don hutawa ko ta zauna falo tayi kallo.

Bakery dinta kau kullum tana samun bayanai akan yadda yake tafiya kuma alhamdullilah sai bunqasa yake.

Wani sa'in idan kadaici ya isheta saita bugama Ummy ta roqeta akan baby tazo.

Duk zuwan da baby keyi bata yarda takai magrib take juyawa, saudart tasha yimata tayin kwana amma firr take qiyawa wai in taganta lahira kaita akayi.


A bangaren ashraf kuwa tuni yakoma bakin aikinsa, dama hutun sati daya ya dauka, shima saboda matsawar sadeeq.


Shi harga Allah wani sa'in mancewa yake da yanada mata, rabonda yasata a idanu tun awajen dinner.

Yasan haqqinshine yasan yaya take ciki dakuma kula da lafiyarshi amma bejin yana iya zuwa ganinta, aganinshi ai ba normal aure bane auren su, auren kwangila ne kowa da dalilinshi nayin auren kuma kowa da abinda yake targeting.






Jera abinci take bisa dining tanayi tana kada kai tana humming tana bin waqar datakeji ta earphones din kunnenta.

Saida ta shirya komai a table din sannan tayi sama tana Dan hadawa da tsalle tsalle Wanda duk acikin shauqin waqar datake jine.

Tana shiga tacire earphones din kunnenta ta fara tu6ewa don watsawa don yau garin badai zafiba, yadda akayi rana yau dakyar idan ba ruwan sama za'ayi ba. Tana gama ty6ewa ta dauki towel ta daura tashige toilet.



Horn yayi sau daya, nan aka shiga scanning din motar, bayan angama gate din ya wangale dakanshi ya kutsa kai yashiga.

A parking space yayi parking sannan yafito ya rufe kofar yayi locking din motar sannan yanufi cikin gida yana sassauta daurin necktie dinshi.

Murda handle din kofar yayi yashiga da sallama, kamar kullum, yauma wannan sanyayyar qamshin da harya fara kama dakin yayi mashi maraba.

Shaqa numfashi yayi ahankali sannan ya fesar, yau qamshin na dabanne don bayan na Wanda dakin yasabayi akwai wani kuma daban Wanda yakasa tantancewa.

Stairs yanufa cikin takunshi na qasaita yana hawa daya bayan daya harya isa sama.

Yauma kamar kodayaushe ko kallon saitin kofar beyiba ya bude kofar shi yashige.

Kasancewar tana toilet tafara wanka duk bataji shigowarshi ba, hasalima tasan lokacin dawowarshi don haka bata kawoma ranta dawowarshi yanzu ba.

Bayan yan mintuna tafito jikinta na digar ruwa, wucewa tayi closet direct don ga yadda ake zafinnan batajin zata iya shafama jikinta komai.

Budewa tayi ta tsaya hannaye riqeda kugu tana bin kayanta dake Jere gwanin kyau da kallo tana shawarar wanne yakamata tasaka.

Ta Dade tana ruwan ido kafin taciro wani three quarter din wando gari mai adon pink din zare a gefe gefen wandon sai mahadinshi wato armless pink vest mai zanen yar Tamar Barbie agaba sannan ta Parke gashinta tsakar kai tayi doughnut dashi sannan tasa wata farar hula marar nauyi.

Turare kawai ta fesa sannan tazura wasu pink baby shoes ta maida earphones dinta ta dauki wayarta tafita.

Harta zauna zata fara serving kanta taji tana sha'awar local lemu, tunawa tayi da lemun tamarin datagani dazu a group, ganin beda wuyar yi yasata tashi tashiga kitchen din don hadoshi.



Tana shiga yafito daga dakin cikin shigar qananun kaya ba Adidas.

Hannunshi daya cikin aljihu dayan kuma riqeda wayar dake kareda kunnenshi alamun waya yake.

A daya daga cikin qayyatatun kujerun falon ya zauna yayi irin balancing dinnan kamar wani Dan sarki ya Dora hannunshi dake cikin aljihu bisa kan kujerar yana cigaba da amsa wayar.


Cikin takunta tafito, hannunta daya riqeda wani haddaden jug, dayan kuma riqeda Glass cup.

Dining tanufa batareda takawoma ranta komai ba.

Serving din kanta tayi cikin plate sannan ta zuba drink din a glass cup tasaka straw aciki sannan ta zauna ta dauki spoon and fork tafara cin abincin cikin nutsuwa.


Tun fitowarta ya bar gane abinda ke wakana a wayar dasuke, da ido yabita tunda tafito har ta isa dining din.

Da farko kasa ganeta yayi, saida ta zauna tana facing dinshi sannan ya wayeta.


Kasa dauke idanu yayi akanta, duk wani motsi nata akan idanunshi, yadda kukasan anhada magnet tsakanin idanunshi da jikinta don kallonta yake bako kyaftawa.

Ita kau a bangarenta batamasan yanayiba don kwata kwata bata kawowa ranta da wani agidan bayan itaba, dukda tana jin alamun idanu akan ta amma bata maida hankali akaiba.


Ringing din wayarta yasata ajiye glass cup din datake tsotsar drink din ta dauki wayar tana duba mai kiran.

Ganin daddy ke kiran yasata katse kiran tana murmushi sannan tasake Kira.

Ta kara a kunne fuskarta fall murmushi sannan ta dauki cup din takai baki tana kur6a.

Kamar ance ta dago, sai caraf idanunshi suka hade.

Wani wawan zuwa tayiwa lemun abinka da tsamiya nan take tahaumata bisa kai tafara tari cikin fitar hayyaci Wanda har tana saukowa qasa...✍

"Yours"

"Wannan dai ko ba'a fadaba nasan na Ummy ne, Ummy gashi"

Ta miqamata.

Sosai saudart taji dadin haka.

Nanfa baby aka dauki wanka aka cake dankwali suka tafi.

Sai wajajen six suka bar gidan bayan mamy tagama kashewa saudart jiki da nasiha.


Direct gidan daddy suka nifa.

Nanfa baby taga tsantsar soyyaya tsakanin uba da diya, fira kau sunsha shi kamar babu gobe.


Koda dasu tafi kuka taitayi dakyar ya rarrasheta yasamu suka tafi.

Haka sukaita fira cikin jindadi har suka isa gidan.

Sosai saudart taji dadin fitarta yau don sosai take jin wani irin nishadi data jima bata jiba.


Parking sukayi suka fito suna dariya.

Can dariyarsu ta tsaya gabadaya a dalilin ganin motar A.A dake fake a parking space din.


"Seems sweetheart dinki nanan" inji baby cikin shaqiyanci.
