038




Washegari saudart bataje bakery ba, tunda tagama aikin gida tayi breakfast ta haye sama.


Bude laptop dinta tayi exactly tafara yan danne dannenta kafin lokacin interview din dazasuyi yayi.


12:00pm suka fara and alhamdullilah tana saka ran samun nasara.


Ranar yini tayi a garden tana aiki a laptop dinta don tana so taqara advancing din bakery dinta ne, tana son ta bude wani qaramin shop kusada bakery din yazama wurin hada variety of ice cream.

Dama ta Dade tana tunani akan hakan, ganin yanzu takeda damar yi kuma kudi ba matsala bane, yin hakan zaisa hanyar shigowar kudinta yaqaru Wanda hakan zaisa ta taimaki dad dinta ya biya duk wani bashi dake wuyanshi.

She loves her Dad soo much, tunda ta taso batasan kowaba sai dad dinta, shaquwar dake tsakanin su baya faduwa,  saboda shi yayi taking din both role dinshi Dana mamanta.

Tun tana yarinya da gari yawaye zaimata duk abinda yakamata uwa tayiwa diyarta.

Wanka, girki, yakaita school, yaje Dakota, suwuce mall dinshi su qarashe yinin tare.

Weekend kuma yakaita wajajen shaqatawa suyini a can kuma yakaita gidan mamanta tayimusu yini daya

Shaquwar da saudart tayi da Daddy ko kwatanta batayi da mamanta ba. Shiyasa matsayinshi ma na daban ne acikin zuciyarta.


Tasan Dad dinta is not perfect, dama kuma duk dan Adam ajizine, shi ajizancinshi shine son kudi.

Duk hanyar dayaga zaisamu yan gidan rana masu tsoka to saiyabi don acewarshi kudi sune komai.

Anan ne ra'ayinsu ya banbanta don ita basu wani dametaba kuma tana qoqarin ganar da daddy hakan amma Wanda yayi nisa ba Lallai bane yaji kira ba.

Shiyasa kullum take sakashi a addu'a don tayi imani cewa addu'a itace takobin mummunai.



Haka tawuni zur a garden din sai wajajen magrib takoma cikin gida tayi hayewarta sama.


Washegari ma batajeba don tunda Dad yanuna 6acin ransa akan hakan taji zuwan duk ya fita kanta.

As usual tagama komai gidan sai daukar qamshi yake, tana kwance tana waya da P.A dinta akan shirye shiryen bude ice cream joint dinta .

Sun dan jima kafin sugama sannan ta kashe wayar.

Kafin ta ajiye wani kiran yashigo.

Ganin daddy ne yasata Sakin murmushi ta kwanta tana maqalqale pillow cikin muryar shagwa6a tace

"Daddy?"

"Na'am shalelen daddy?"

Turo baki tayi tace "daddy I miss you"

"Miss you more baby, shine baki gayamin ba?"

"Menene?"

"Really? Bakima saniba?"

"Menene to dad? Kafadamin kawai"

"To albishirinki"

Cikin zaquwa tace "goro fari"


"You're employed!"

Waro idanunta tayi cikin jindadi

"Da gaske daddy?"

"Eh mana, yanzu muka gama magana da P.A din companyn"


"Wow dad, that's soo cool, naji dadi" tafada da murmushi a fuskarta dukda bawani farinciki takeyi canba.

"And guess what?"

"What?"

Ta amsa tana buga tagumi da hannu daya.


"A matsayin secretary aka daukeki a company din"

Waro idanu tasakeyi tana cewa

"Really dad?"

,"sosaima, with a sum of 250k duk wata"

Sake ware idanu tayi

"Wow! Wow!! Dad am speechless!"

Dariya Alhaji shamsu yayi mata, I told you? Ina gwadamaki annabi kina rufe idanu. Idan kika cigaba da yimin biyyaya zakiga fin haka, zakiyi bala'in kudi"

"Hmm zan daiyi kudi masu albarka dad, ba na bala'i ba"

Ta6e baki yayi yace 

"Whatever, yanzu ki shirya zaki fara zuwa ranar Monday ne, please you have to be serious kuma kinsan I love you ko? Kuma bazan ta6a cutar dakeba"

"Yes, I know"

"Kuma kinsan komai nakeyi saboda ke nakeyi, banida kowa banida family bayan ke kuma banida mai farantamin bayan ke ko?"

Dan daga gira tayi alamun tambaya 

"Eh dad, amma meya kawo wannan maganar? You know I love you so much, farincikinka shine nawa, shiyasa ma zanyi wannan aikin domin taimaka maka wajen ganin ka sauke duk wani nauyi dake kanka"


"Eh nasani dear, saidai kiyimin alqawari bazakiyi disappointing dinaba, zaki qar6i aikin nan duk yadda kikaga yazo miki"

Shiru tayi na dan lokaci kafin tace 

"Ban ganeba dad, is something wrong with the job?"

"No, absolutely no, kawai I want you to accept it ne duk yadda kika ganshi"

Ajiyar zuciya tayi tace

"Zanyi amma sai idan be sa6ama addiniba"

Cikin jindadi yace

"Yes na tabbata miki be sa6ama addiniba, wlh"

"To Allah yayimana jagora"

"Amin my jewel, Allah ya albarkaci rayuwarki"

Cikin jindadi tace "amin Abby"




Kingin ranakun tashiga busy sosai wajen ganin ta ice cream joint din ya kafu.


Kwana uku ana aikin kafin agama kuma alhamdullilah komai yatafi mata yadda takeso.

Ranar asabar aka bude wajen kuma tadanyi taro babu laifi akayi addu'a samun sa'a akaci akasha sannan aka watse.

Nanfa ta duqufa wajen ganin komai yatafi kan tsari.

Ice cream babu kalar da basu saidawa, acikin su akwai na vanilla, chocolate flavour, strawberry flavour, banana flavour ddss.

Alhaji shamsu kau ya dauki nauyin tallatar mata da wajen ta kafar yad'a labarai wato t.v, radio da social media.

Duk wannan abun da akeyi Ashraf na sane amma ko nuna yasan sunayi beyiba, to tayama zai nuna bayan haduwarsu ma aikine.

Kowa zaman kanshi yake a gidan so babu Wanda yadamu da abinda dan uwanshi ke ciki.


Su Ummy kau basuda masaniya akai saida suka gani a t.v  ana talla, nan baby ta kirata tana tambayar dagaske ita ta bude.

Da eh saudart ta amsamata, sosai baby tayi murna wai likafarta taci gaba, dama ita mayyar ice cream ce, duk sadda taji kwadayi zatazo ta jidi son ranta.

Dariya saudart tayi tana cewa babu damuwa ai kayan Allah na annabi ne.





***********************************

Yau Monday, tunda wuri ta tashi tayi abubuwan data sabayi dasafe ta hada breakfast dinta taci sannan tashiga wanka.


Wajajen takwas da Rabi harta gama shirinta tsabb cikin wata sky blue din Arabian gown bubu Wanda yaji duwatsu masu daukar idanu daga gaban rigar.
Ta yane kanta da veil mai dan girma sky blue Wanda ya kawomata har saman ciki.

Ta rataya jakka baqa sai takalmi masu dan tsini baqaqe hannunta kuma daure da agogo kamfanin Apple baqa a hannu.

Fuskarta babu wata kwalliya bayan powder da kwallin data sakama idanunta sai lashes dinta data sharce da mascara, shikenan.

Bata fesa turare mai uban qamshi ba, mai sanyayan qamshi tafesa Wanda saikazo kusada ita zaka jishi.

Jin horn a waje yasata gane drivern da daddy yace zai turomata ya qaraso.

Saka wayarta da abubuwan amfani tayi a jakkar tasake kallon kanta a madubi tana gyara daurin veil din sannan tafito.

Da sauri ta sauko tana sake duba time tanufi hanyar fita.

Saurin bude kofar tayi tasaka kai zatafita sai quuum!  Suka qume dajuna.

Ba qarya sun qumu don saida suka ja da baya suna Sosa wajen suna kallon juna.


Ganin beda niyyar tankamata ko matsawa yasata ra6awa ta gefenshi zata wuce.

Sai jitayi an chafki tsintsiyar hannunta an maidata baya da qarfi Wanda saida kafarta ta haggu ta murgude tayi baya baya zata fadi Allah ya taimaka ta dafe shoe shelves dake wajen.

Dagowa tayi a firgice tana kallonshi don bata ta6a zaton hakaba awajenshi.

Shima kallonta yake fuska a hade yana kallon direct tsakiyar kwayar idonta.

"Ke makauniya ce?  You hit me and you're going without saying sorry? Dole ne saikin gwada bakida manners? Well unfortunately nasani, nasan you're ill-mannered before I even get to know you"


Kasa cewa komai tayi sai kallonshi datake ga wani daci datake ji cikin maqoshinta jin ya kirata marar manner.

"Kina sauri zaki yawon tazubar ko? Well I don't fucking care ina zaki, kawai don't drag my good name to mud, don a matsayin Matar A'A kike ga mutane, behave yourself karki kuskure mutunci na ya ta6u a idon jama'a"

Yayimata wani kallon up and down sannan yawuce ciki yabarta nan tsaye.


Bata waigo ta kalleshiba dayake wucewa, zuciyarta takeji namata wani irin zafi kamar ana hura garwashi aciki.

Muquut.. Ta hadiye yawu mai daci daya taru abakinta ta gyara rolling din veil dinta jin ansake yin horn.

Bude kofar tayi ta fita asanyaye ranta a matuqar 6ace, tafito har wajen gate wajen drivern daya zo daukarta tabude bayan seat ta zauna.

Cikin fara'a drivern yace
"Sannu da isowa hajiya" 
Don dama akwai kyakyawar alaqa tsakanin ta da tan aikinsu don lafiya tana wasa da dariya dasu.

Yaqe tayi tace "yauwa bala, ya aiki?"

Da alhamdullilah ya amsa daga nan kuma babu Wanda yasake magana.

Shiru tayi abaya tana sauraron tafiyar motarsu a kwalta, yayinda abinda yafaru yanzu ke dawomata.


Babu abinda yafi bata haushi kamar marar manner daya kirata.

Itadai tasan qumewa sukayi kuma both of them sunji zafin, why zaiyi insulting dinta?


Wannan na cikin abubuwan dayasa tun farko take qauracewa ganinshi, a duniya idan akwai abinda ta tsana to cin mutunci ne amma batun yauba ta lura ya qware akan hakan shiyasa ma batason haduwarsu don bazata iya dauka ba, tafison har ta qaraci zamanta su rabu babu abinda yashiga tsakaninsu daidai da maganar fatar baki.

Jin an tsaya ana horn yasata sauke ajiyar zuciya tana kauda tunaninta don yaune ranar farkonta a aiki yakamata tazama tana cikin nutsuwarta.


Direct parking space yayi daita sannan yasamu wuri yayi parking.

Ajiyar zuciya tasake saki tana addu'ar farawa a sa'a sannan tasa hannu ta bude murfin kofar tafito.


Abinda tagani ne yasa numfashinta  daukewa na wuccen gadi....✍

039



Mitsitsike idanunta tayi taqara kallon wajen don tabbatar da ba idanunta kemata gizo ba amma still wajen ne, companyn ne.

Juyawa tayi wajen bala dake niyyar yin reverse tace

"Bala ka tabbatar nan ne inda Dad yace ka kawoni?"

Cikin yashe baki yace "eh hajiya, nan ne"


Sauke numfashi tayi tana dafa goshinta tareda lumshe idanu.

*kiyimin alqawari bazakiyi disappointing dinaba, zaki qar6i aikin nan duk yadda kikaga yazo miki*

Maganar dad na jiya yadawo mata a qwanya.

"Why dad? Why?"


"Hajiya? Lafiya dai ko?" Inji bala daketa kallonta tundazu.

Bude idanunta dasuka fara canza launi tayi ta kalleshi tama kasa magana.


"You're welcome Mrs A.A" Sukaji anfada daga bayan su.

Juyawa sukayi gabadaya suna kallon mai maganar.

Sadeeq ne ya qaraso yana washe baki yana cewa

"You're highly welcome ma'am, mushiga ciki mana"

Kallonshi tayi sannan ta daga kai tana bin company din da kallo batareda ta bayyanar da yanayin datake aciki ba a fuska ta sake maida kallonta kan sadeeq tasaki murmushin takaici sannan tajuya ta fara kiciniyar bude motar dasukazo daita.

"Erm.. Mrs A.A please listen to me, atleast mufara shiga ciki inmiki bayani"

Banza tayi dashi ta bude kofar zata shiga 

"Mrs A.A..."

"A.A my foot! Karka sake dangantani da sunan nan" tafada a fusace

"Amma wannan ne company din dazaki..."

"Fuck the company!" Tafada tana jawo murfin motar da qarfi.

Tsawa ta dakama bala akan yashigo sutafi, aikau dagudu ya bude motar yashiga ya tada suka fice.

"Shit!" Sadeeq yafada yana riqeda kugu.





Gudu bala keta tsulawa batareda yasan inda zashiba saidai kuma yana tsoron tambayarta don yasan idan tayi fushi akan kowama hucewa take duk yadda kau kuke daita.

Can dai ya sadaqat yace
"Ranki shi Dade ina zamu?"

Wani kallo ta watsa mashi ta glass din gaba Wanda hakan yasashi maida hankalinshi kan tukin

Can kamar bazata yi magana ba tace
"Daddy.. Take me to him"

Dukda besan me tace daga bayaba jin ta ambaci daddy yasashi sanin wajen shi zaya kaita.


Jingina kanta tayi da kujera ta lumshe ido tana sauraron yadda zuciyarta ke zafi.

Meyasa dad a duniya bayada burin da yawuce ya zubarmata da mutunci?

Meyasa dad beda burin daya wuce ya quntata mata?

Meyasa yacika son kanshi?

Yarasa inda zai nemomata aiki sai wannan companyn?

Wane irin kallo yakeson suyimata?


Jin motar ta tsaya yasata bude idanu tana kallon mall din sannan tasa hannu ta bude murfin kofar tafito.


Shiga mall din tayi direct tanufi office din babbanta batareda tako tankama masu yimata magana ba.

Murda handle din kofar tayi ta bude tashiga batareda ko sallama ba.

Wanda hakan yasa daddy da wani mutum dasuke tattaunawa tare dagowa suna kallonta.

Batace komai ba ta qarasa gefen office din dake akwai cushion ta zauna ta zaro waya tana danne danne.

Maida hankalinshi dad yayi kan mutumin suka cigaba da tattaunawa har suka gama suka tashi sukayi musabaha mutumin yafita.

Kallon wajen saudart yayi yaga haryanzu bata dago daga kan danne dannen datakewa wayarba.

Wani irin murmushin manya yayi yanufi fridge din office din ya Ciro ruwan gora da glass cup ya qaraso ya zauna kusada ita ya tsiyaya mata a cup yabata.

Hannu tasa ta amsa batareda ta kalleshi ba ta kafa kai tasha kusan Rabi sannan ta ajiye.

Shiru office din ya dauka, kowannensu beda niyyar magana.

 Kamo hannunta daya yayi yana murzawa ahankali yana kallonta itakau haryanzu idanunta na bisa wayar hannunta.

"Am sorry" yafada cikin rada.

Lumshe idanu tayi zuciyarta na cigaba da tafasa.

"Saudart nasan a halin yanzu kin tsaneni, kuma na cancanci haka, nasan am not a good father, ina yawan 6atamiki rai, ina yawan saki a damuwa...saidai banida yadda na iya ne"

Qara damke hannunta yayi cikin sigar dadin baki daya qware akai yace
"Banida kowa saike, banida uwa, banida uba, banida mata, banida 'ya'ya bayan ke, ke kadai zan iya samun sassauci awajen ki, ke kadai zaki iya taimaka min, ke kadai nakedashi dazan iya dazan iya fadawa damuwa ta inkuma saka ran zaki taimaka min, wataqila da na haifi wasu da ban takuramaki dayawa ba, da nasan akwai Wanda zai tausayamin aciki, da akwai Wanda zai iya jure komai akan samun farinciki na"


Haryanzu idanunta a lumshe suke saidai in banda hawaye babu abinda ke gangarowa daga cikin lumsassun idanunta.sosai maganar daddy ke shiga direct cikin zuciyarta tana narketa kamar yadda ake narke darma.

Wai yau daddy yakejin inama yanada wasu yaran bayan ita? 

Sosai abun ya ta6amata zuciya.

"It ok saudart, nasan kinzo nan ne don kice bazakiyi aiki a company din ba, babu komai, zan cigaba da Neman yadda zanyi in hada kudin, koda ban hadaba idan wa'adin yacika zan saida mall din saina bashi kudin kingin kuma saina samu wata yar Sana'a nayi... It ok kinji? Kibar kukan hakan, I love you, Allah yamiki albarka"


Tashi yayi zai tafi yaji ta riqomashi hannu Wanda hakan yasashi tsayawa batareda ya juyoba.

Idonta still a lumshe ta bude bakinta dakyar tace

"Aiki a company din zai sakaka farinciki?"

Juyawa yayi yana kallonta yace

"A'a shalele, I want your happiness, don't worry"

Bude idanunta tayi tana kallonshi da idanunta dasuka ida rinewa sannan ahankali tasake cewa
"Zai sakaka farinciki?"

Shiru yayi yana kallonta kafin yace
"Eh saudart, babu company dazamu samu mai biyan albashi mai tsoka kamar wannan, kuma..."

"It ok" ta katseshi da fadin haka sannan ta tashi tsaye tana gyara nadin gyalenta ta dauki Jakarta tayi hanyar kofa. Yabita da kallo 


Harta sa hannu zata bude kofar muryarshi ta dakatar da ita.

"Shalele.."

"Ina sonka, kaine silar zuwana duniya ko me nayimaka bazan biyaka, bazan so naganka cikin damuwa ba bayan inada maganinta, bazan so a dalilinaba kayi danasani ko kukan Rashin 'ya'ya dayawa ba, zan iya sadaukar da farincikina kamar yadda kasha sadaukar da naka wajen samamaka farinciki.
Saidai... Saidai karka yi tunanin zaka iya sani sa6awa Allah na bayan wadda kasani nayi abaya, idan dagaske saboda na taimaka maka wajen biyan bashin kanka yasa ka nemomin aiki fine, amma idan kanada wata manufa akan haka saidai kayi haquri, wata qila anan zan Gaza sama maka farinciki"

Tana kaiwa nan tabude kofar tafice.


Alhaji shamsu yadade nan a tsaye yana bin inda tabi tawuce da kallo.

Sai yanzu yafara tuhumar kanshi akan anya yayi mata adalci? Anya kalaman dayayi amfani dasu basuyi tsauriba, yasan saudart batada wani Wanda takeso takeson sashi a farinciki bayan shi, meyasa yayi amfani da wadannan kalaman wajen karya mata zuciya.

Komawa yayi ya zauna yana jin badadi har cikin zuciyarshi.





Key din motar ta amsa hannun bala ta bude motar tashiga ta tada sannan tafice daga harabar mall din.


Tafiya take hawaye na gangaro mata duk kau kokarin datake na tsaidasu.

Ba komai kesata hawaye ba sai kalaman dad na inama yanada wasu yaran, wannan Kalmar tafimata ciwo kuma tasan zata Dade tana cimata zuciya.


Ikon Allah kawai ya kaita company din lfy.

Parking tayi a parking space sannan takoma ta jingina da seat din tana lumshe idanu.

"Ya Allah give me strength"

Ganin zaman be yiwuwa yasata budewa ta zuro kafafunta tafito waje.


Sake kallon harabar company din tayi tana tuna farkon zuwanta company din dakuma abinda yafaru a ranar.


Maida murfin kofar tayi tarufe sannan tafara takawa jiki a sanyaye tanufi main entrance din.

Wajen wanke hannu taje ta matsa sanitizer tafara wanke hannun yayinda komai na farkon zuwanta company din ke dawomata a qwanya.

Danna botton din kofar tayi yabude tashiga sannan yakoma yarufe sannan daga can ciki kuma yabude tashiga.

Daidaikun mutane taga sunata kai kawo kamar dai ranan kowa da abinda yasha mashi kai.


Direct wajen elevator tanufa ta Danna number din floor din sannan tashiga.

Cikin yan daqiqu sai jitayi abun ya tsaya sai kofar tabude.

Shiru tayi tana kallon wajen batareda ta fitoba gabanta sai bugu yake.

Ganin elevator din zai koma yarufe yasata sauke wata nannauyan ajiyar zuciya sannan ta zuro kafarta tafito.


Kamar wancan karon, qamshi da sanyi yafara yimata maraba, babu abinda ya canza daga yadda yake lokacin datazo sai empty kujerar secretary data gani babu kowa akai Wanda yanzu ita zata dinga zama akai.


Ta Dade tsaye tana qarewa wajen kallo batareda tayi yinkurin motsawa ba taji a bude kofa an fito.

Saurin waigawa tayi suka hada ido.

Washe baki yasakeyi.

"There you are! Sanni dazuwa Mrs A.. I mean saudart, ga wajen ki can, muje please"

Babu musu tabishi ya budemata tashiga, wajen rufe yake da glass don haka kana hangen naciki kuma koda zaka ba nawaje Abu akwai inda zaka zuge ka fidda abun batareda ka fitoba ko na wajen ya shigo.


Bin office din take da kallo cikin takaici, don duk qawatuwar wajen be burgeta ba.

Sadeeq sai zuba yake yana nunnunamata abubuwa yana mata bayani itakau tana gefe ta rungume hannuwa a qirjinta tana saurarenshi.

Saida yakai aya sannan yace

"Erm.. Yanzu wadancan files din zaki kaima boss yayi signing" yafada a darare.


Jimm tayi kamar bazata motsaba saikuma can ta sauke ajiyar zuciya ta matso kan desk din dake cike da files da computoci tace

"Wadanne files?"

Tattaramata su yayi yabata tayi mashi godiya sannan yafice.

Itama fitowa tayi daga office din tanufi office din.

Daga kai tayi ta kalli abinda aka rubuta sama

*the c.e.o office*

Ta Dade tsaye awajen tana yunkurin shiga saikuma ta fasa.

Da ace mutuwarta zatazo a lokacin koko ta 6ace 6att datafi murna.

Yau zatayi facing dinshi a matsayin boss dinta, ita kuma a matsayin secretary dinshi, wannan wane irin zubarda mutunci ne?

Tunawa tayi da abinda yafaru dasafe kafin tabaro gidan, kenan don yasan zatazo office dinshi yasashi yimata hakan, no wonder, dama tayi mammaki, tunda sukayi aure magana ta fatar baki bata ta6a hadasuba sai yau, kenan saboda yasan zatazo company dinshi a matsayin mai mashi aiki yasa yayi hakan?


Idan hakane to ya tanadar mata cin mutuncin dayafi hakan kenan.

Ca6, Lallai, zata iya jurar komai amma banda cin fuska, bazata ta6a barinshi ya maida ta abun wulanqatawa ba.

Shaqar numfashi tayi da qarfi sannan ta fesar sannan ta daga hannu tafara knocking.


Sai ana ukun sannan taji ance

"Yes? Come in"


Gabanta ne ya tsananta bugu, hannunta na dan 6ari ta murda handle din kofar ta bude...✍

(Ummin fasihu)





040




Tattaro sauran jarumtarta tayi ta tura kofar tashiga kamar Wanda kwai yafashe mawa aciki.

Babu abinda ya canza a office din, yananan yadda ta sanshi tun farkon zuwanta.

Qasa qarasawa tayi taja ta tsaya a bakin kofar zuciyarta na dukan Tara Tara.

Jitake kamar qasa ta bude ta hadiyeta ta huta.

Wannan zubarda mutunci dame yayi kama?

Duk abinda A.A yayimata tabbass ita ta siya da kudinta, da wane ido zata kalleshi? Dawane ido zai kalleta? Yaya zai fassarata?

Jin shirun yayi yawa yasata dagowa Tadan saci kallonshi taga kanshi na kan system bemada niyyar dagowa.

Ajiyar zuciya ta sauke sannan ta ida tattaro kingin kuzarinta ta qarasa cikin office din.

"Good morning" tafada cikin nutsuwa

Cak ya tsaya da typing din dayake yakasa cigaba saboda muryarta datayi mashi dirar mikiya a kunnuwa.

Dora files din tayi saman table din sannan tace
"I was told to bring these files to you, your signature is needed" tafada cikin nutsuwa amma deep down she's dying.

Juyawa tayi saurin yi tanufi hanyar kofa.

Dagowa yayi yana kallonta, saidai harta kusa kaiwa bakin kofar, hakan yasashi dakatar daita da

"Wait!"

Cak ta tsaya tana runtse idanu da qarfi zuciyarta kamar zata Faso qirjinta ta fito dan bugawa.

Ganin batada niyyar juyowa yasashi cewa

"Who are you?"

Yawun bakinta taji ya qafe jitake kamar ta 6ace 6att daga office din.
Dakyar ta tattaro yawu a bakinta ta hadiye sannan cikin calm voice tace
"Am your new secretary"

Yes itace, tabbass muryarta ce, bazai ta6a Qin gane muryarta ba, kallon bayanta yake don still bata juyoba, dukda be cika qaremata kallo ba amma still yasan wannan jikin, jikinta ne.

Ganin ta cigaba da tafiya zata fita yasashi cewa
"Stop!" Da qarfi.

Ja tayi ta tsaya again batareda ta juyoba.
Cikin qufula yace "come back here!"

Anzo wajen! Dama abinda take Gudu kenan, facing dinshi, bataji tana iya facing dinshi, her emotions won't let her.

Hawaye taji suna Neman tarrarmata a idanu tayi saurin maidasu, tayiwa kanta alqawari duk rintsi bazata ta6a barinshi yaga weak point dinta ba.

Juyowa tayi ahankali ta kalleshi suka hada idanu.

Dumm.. Gabansu yafadi gabadaya yayinda Ashraf yayi mutuwar zaune awajen yana kallonta baki bude.


Qarasowa tayi har gaban table dinshi fuska ba yabo ba fallasa tana kallonshi

"What! W..what the hell are you doing here?"

Fuskarta normal batareda ta bayyana yanayin datake cikiba tace
"Sorry, banyi introducing kainaba, I'm miss saudart shamsu by name, your new secretary" tafada cikin mugun wayancewa yadda kasan yau dama tafara saninshi.

Sagale yayi da baki yana kallonta don he's totally speechless ma.

Batareda ta nuna damuwa da tsaretan dayayi da idanu ba ta cigaba dacewa

"Today is my first day, guess I have a lot to handle, zanje in hada scheme of work"

Tana kaiwa nan tajuya tanufi qofa cikin takunta.
Kasa tsaidata yayi harta fita.

What!
What the hell is going on?

Hannu na 6ari ya jawo landline din dake kan table dinshi ya daddana lambobin landline din office din sadeeq.


Fita tayi ta rufo kofar ta jingina daita hannunta dafe da qirjinta tana numfashi sama sama.

Ita kadai tasan jarumtar datayi wajen facing din Ashraf.
This is the toughest time ever in her life.

Saida tagama dawowa daidai sannan tamiqe daga jikin kofar ta wuce jiki a sanyaye office dinta ta bude tashiga.


Tsayawa tayi tanabin tsararren office din da kallo Wanda desk din dake daga gefe cike yake da computoci ga files files da scripts agefe ajere gwanin sha'awa.

Tsaki taja don babu abinda ya burgeta aciki, ta qaraso ta zauna akan kujerar dake facing din desk din.









Ringing din landline din ya dakatar dashi daga rubuce rubucen dayake.

Saurin toshe baki yayi yana qumshe dariya ganin boss ke kira.
Saida ya daidaita nutsuwarshi sannan ya daga wayar.

"Hello?"


"Get the hell here! Now!"

Ding.. Aka katse kiran.

Murmushi sadeeq yayi don dama yasan za'a Rina.


Tashi yayi ya gyara suit dinshi sannan yafito.




Taga fitowarshi amma saita kauda kau ta fara plugging din socket din system din tanayi tana kallonshi qasa qasa harya shige office din.



Da sallama yashiga office din.
Ganin yanayin fuskar Ashraf yasashi kusan kecewa da dariya, mazewa yayi ya qaraso cikin office din.


"Good morning s..."


"Kaga riqe gaisuwarka Mr man, what the hell did you think you're doing?" Yafada cikin daga murya

"Menene..."

"Don't dare ask me menene! Kafini sanin dalilin zuwanka nan" yasake katseshi a fusace

"Sir.."

"Don't sir me! Ka Kirani da Ashraf dina mallam, ubanwa yasaka daukarta?!" Yafada cikin tada jijiyoyin wuya.


"Ashraf..."

"Just shut up! Yanzu kaje ka rubuta mata takardar sallama, she's fired!"

"What! Ashraf meye haka? Atleast ka saurareni"

"Nagama magana, she's fired"

"Amma..."

"Ammo! Get out!"

"A.A..."

"Out!!"


Shiru sadeeq yayi yana kallonshi cikin ido da alamu shima yafara fusata.

"Me kake jira? I said out!"

"Bazan fitaba! Zoka fiddani idan ka isa! Why zaka dinga yimin tsawa? Who did you think you are?!" Yafada shima cikin daga murya


"Atleast ka tsaya ka saurareni mana, kwana biyu da yad'a vacancy letter babanta yakirani akan na dauketa aikin,  I was shocked nima a lokacin amma daga baya naga ai muma wani opportunity ne garemu na tracking dinshi
Nasan yanada wata manufa bayan dalilin daya karantomin na daukarta, he thought bamu sanshi bane, he thought bamusan me yake qullawaba ne.
Wannan itace the easiest and the fastest means na cimmashi.

I thought kaima cunkusashen kwakwalwarka zata baka haka amma am mistaken" ya qarshe zancen yana makamashi mugun kallo


"Koma menene bazan iya aiki da wannan aljanar yarinyar ba"

"Ita waya ce maka dason ranta tazo? She's forced kamar yadda aka tilastamata wajen qaddararen auren ka, bayan haka ko kallo baka isheta ba kaima kasani, kuma kafin ka kira wani da aljani kafara duba mirror"


"Hey watch your words! Am still your boss"

"Boss my ass! Nabi boss dagudu, idiot" yafada yana nufar kofa

"Kaje nayi suspending dinka saina nemeka"

"Sai kazo ka fiddani din, mtcheew" ya fita yana bugo kofar da qarfi.

Bin qofar yayi da kallo, yasan sadeeq yakai bango ne, shi dama be iya zuciya ba, kamar yadda yakeda wuyar zama haka yakeda wuyar sauka.

Tsaki yaja yakoma ya zauna yana huci.




Jin anbude kofa yasata dagowa, gani tayi sadeeq ne yafito daga office din.

Ta6e baki tayi ta kauda kai.

Kamar zai wuce saikuma yadawo yayi knocking akan glass door dinta ya tura yashigo.

Ko dagowa batayiba bare ta kalleshi, typing kawai take cikin qwarewa.

"Is everything alright? Ko akwai wata matsala?"

Batareda ta kalleshi ba idanunta akan screen din computer tace "No" ataqaice

Be sake cewa komai ba yajuya yafita don ya lura itama yar shan qamshice na bugawa a news.


Da harara tabishi don shima haushi yake bata ba kadan ba.


Cikin qwarewa ta tsara scheme din sannan tafara printing din appointment letters datagani tili guda a email har tana mammakin uwar me zaiyi musu da zasuyita bankomashi wasiqar Neman izinin ganinshi.


Saida tayi printing din sha biyar tana bi according to the date, sannan tsagaita hakanan ta duba agogo taga daya saura.

Tattara takardun tayi ta tashi tafita ta nufi kofarshi badan ranta yaso ba.

Sau biyu tayi knocking amma babu amsa hakan yasa ta murda handle din kofar ta shiga da sallama.

Yana zaune kan kujerarshi ya aza gwiwar hannun damanshi dake riqeda Biro bisa table yana taunar murfin biron ahankali.

Tunda tashigo ya kafeta da idanu harta qaraso gaban table din cikin salon tafiyarta.

Dukda ta taqura matuqa da tsareta da idanun dayayi hakan besa tanuna ba.

Qarasowa gaban table din tayi taga ko ta6a files din dazu beyiba.

Dora takardun hannunta tayi kan table din

"This is the scheme" tafada tana turamashi.

"And these are some of the appointment letters, the one to be attended should be indicated, naga wasu harda na last week, there are two meetings tomorrow ma, daya joint meeting ne na Adams &co. Company, dayan kuma partnership meeting, gasunan dai a wannan takardar" tafada tana turamashi takardar.

Shidai tsayawa yana kallonta yadda tawani yi fuska tana kwararo zance.

Batareda tasake cewa komai ba ta juya tafara tafiya.

"Wow! Bravo" yafada yana tafa hannayenshi.

Cakk ta tsaya bugun zuciyarta na tsananta.

"So? Are you this shameless?... Nasan kunya gaba kuka bata ba bayaba amma ban ta6a tunanin Rashin kunyr harta Kai hakaba"

Jitayi jinin jikinta na kafewa yayinda wani daci daci ke ziyartar maqoshinta...✍


Ummin fasihu ce🧚‍♀

041



Jitayi jinin jikinta na kafewa yayinda wani daci daci ke ziyartar maqoshinta.


"Are you that desperate?" Yafada yana takowa inda take tsaye bata juyoba.

"Idan ban mantaba a company dinnan, a office dinnan, a rana irin ta yau, kika bude baki kikace ban isheki kalloba bare abinda na mallaka, you don't care who I am and my personality.

Ya akayi kuma yanzu? Abin mammaki yau the proud peacock ce a gabana amatsayin secretary na...you shouldn't have stooped so low, basai kin qasqantar da kanki ba wajen cin kudina, you have the right.
Da kin tambayeni ko nawa kikeso zan baki kodan darajar wannan tsararren auren namu, amma it's a shame, an extreme shame ace diyar shamsu, the mighty Saudart herself tayi stooping low wajen zama secretary na... *koba hakaba?*" yaqarashe maganar cikin rad'a yana kafeta da hazal eyes dinshi kasancewar ya zagayo gabanta suna kallon juna.

Wani siririn murmushi tasaki ta kalleshi taga shima fuskarshi dauke take da murmushin gefen baki Wanda yafi kama da na mugunta.


"Isn't that obvious Mr A.A?" Tafada still murmushi a fuskarta.

"Ba qasqantar dakai bane, it's called *BUSINESS*"

Daga gira daya yayi still yana kallonta murmushin kuma bebar fuskarshi ba.

"A tunanina a matsayinka na dan kasuwa yakamata kasan the full meaning of *BUSINESS*, wannan ba qasqantar dakai bane, *BUSINESS* ne, *HALAQ* dinane, my sweat.
Me kake tunani? A matsayina na yar kasuwa, diyar yan kasuwa, babana shahararren dan kasuwa ne, mamana shahararriyar yar dealer ce, duk abinda nasan zai kawomin samu muddin halaq ne zan yishi.
Am a real hustler, I hustle day and night so far it's halaq, bana depending akan wani, bana jiran abun wani, bana kwadayin abun wani saboda be dameni ba, inacin guminane, haqqina, same goes with this, aiki zanyi kuma a biyani, I don't care" tafada tana daga kafadu🤷‍♀

"Batun aure kuma Kai kema tunawa dashi har kake ganin zanci darajarshi, as far as am concerned ni ba Matar kowa bace, karka manta it's all contract, signed contract.

So am here for business ne kawai, bansanka ba, baka sanniba, babu wani alaqa tsakaninmu saina boss da employee dinshi, bayan wannan kuma babu wani dangantakar... *koba hakaba?*" itama ta qarshe maganar cikin rad'a.



Murmushin da beyi niyyar yi bane ya subucemashi yadan kawar dakai yanayi.

Lallai wannan yarinyar, her courage, her pride da confidence dinta yayi yawa.
Da watace dauko dago kai ta kalleshi bazata iyaba, da watace da yanzu tananan tanaji kamar ta nitse don kunya amma banda ita, banda shugabbar yan girman kai din duk duniya. 
This is an opportunity, damarshice na koyamata hankali, na koyamata yadda ake girmama na gaba.

"Nice one miss Saudart, business ne ya kawoki right? Babu wani dangantaka tsakaninmu saina boss damai aikin shi, good and so be it, let the business start"


Saikuma ya matso dab daita har suna shaqar numfashin juna, idanunshi cikin nata.

"But are you sure you can cope with a boss like me?"

Dukda yadda takeji na yanayin kusancinsu ta danne tace "is this a challenge?"

Cikin rad'a yace "yes"

Murmushi ta qaqaro Wanda bekai zuciba tace
"Challenge.. Accepted"itama cikin rad'ar.

Murmushin gefen baki yayi yana kallonta, itama samun kanta tayi da d'an rausayar da kanta gefe itama dauke da irin murmushin shi.


Jada baya yadanyi still idanunsu cikin juna sannan yajuya yanufi desk dinshi.

Wasu takardu dogaye ya kwaso batareda yasan adadinsu ba yadawo gabanta ya dorasu saman table kusada ita.

Batace komaiba sai kallon takardun datayi sannan ta maida kallonta akanshi alamun qarin bayani.

" kiyi copy dinsu, kiyi printing sannan kowane guda daya ayi photocopy dinshi waje goma...Good luck " ya qarshe zancen yana komawa mazauninshi ya zauna yayi balancing Yana binta da wani irin kallo.

"With pleasure" tafada da murmushi sannan ta tattare takardun tafice.

Binta yayi da kallo harta fita, wani irin haushi yakeji azuciyarshi, wai me yarinyar nan ke taqama dashi ne? Me ta dauki kanta ne? Soyayi yayimata wankin babban bargo yau amma daga qarshe shi ta cusama haushin.

Qwafa yayi yana jinjina kai, zan koyamiki hankali ne.




Itakau tana shiga office dinta ta ajiye takardun saman desk dinta ta shige toilet dake cikin office din.

Ahankali ta qarasa gaban sink din toilet din ta bude fanfon wajen ta Tara tattausan tafin hannayenta ruwan na zuba cikinsu tana kallo.
Biji biji tafara gani sanadiyar hawayen dasuka tararmata acikin idanu.

Barinsu tayi suka gangaro batareda tayi yunqurin tsaidasu ba.

Tun tana hawaye harta fara shesheka ahankali.

Zafi takeji acikin zuciyarta kamar ana ruramata wuta, ga wata wutar Qin Ashraf dake ruruwa a zuciyarta, ga takaicin abinda daddy yayimata dazu, Abu dai yazaman mata goma da ashirin.


Saida taci kukanta ta qoshi sannan ta wanke fuskarta da ruwan fanfon ta tsane fuskarta da hand towel.

Dagowa tayi ta kalli kanta ta cikin mirror dake jikin sink din taga idanunta dama fuskarta sunyi jajur.
Murmushin takaici tayi sannan ta daura alwala tafito.


Dayake tazo da spare hijab a Jakarta dama, veil dinta ta warware ta samu qusurwa ta shinfida, dayake Allah yamata baiwar gane gabbas duk inda ta tsinci kanta, down haka shimfidawa tayi ta zura hijabi ta gabatar da sallar zuhr, tayi addu'o'inta sannan ta miqe tacire hijabin ta yafa veilbdinta qaraso gaban desk dinta.

Takardun daya bata ta dauka tafara dubawa.

Gabanta ne yafadi ganin uban aikinda yasata.
Takardun qwara shabiyar dogaye kowanne an rubuceshi gaba da baya, tasan intayi gudun tsiya tayi copy din biyu cikin awa daya, kafin a kaiga printing ga kuma photocopy.

Jitayi wasu sabbin hawaye na zuwamata, saurin maidasu tayi tana girgiza ksi
'No saudart, ba yanzu ba, you're strong, be strong'

Jan kujerar gaban desk din tayi ta zauna ta zari paper daya tafara aikin.


Aiki take tuquru batareda shiriritaba, babu abinda ke tadata sai sallah, tama manta dawani Abu waishi abinci, kodama ta tuna batajin tana iya sama cikinta wani Abu.


Qarfe shidda saura kofar office din Ashraf ta bude ya fito hannunshi daya riqeda briefcase dayan kuma sa6e da jacket din suit dinshi.

Taji fitowarshi kuma tasan shine amma ko dago kanta batayiba bare ta nuna tasan da wanzuwarshi.

Shima ko gefenta be kallaba yawuce private elevator dinshi da shi kadai ke ya Danna floor din qarshe kofar ta bude yashige.



Sai bakwai saudart tafito daga company din, shima bawai tagama aikin bane.
Tadaiyi copy din duka tayi printing dinsu, photocopy kawai yarage Wanda ta aje da niyyar shine Abu na farko dazatayi gobe idan Allah ya kaimu.

Agajiye tashiga motarta tarufe tafice daga company din, saida ta tsaya restaurant tayi takeaway taje pharmacy ta siya maganin ciwon jiki sannan tanufi gida.

Agajiye ta qarasa gida, sallar magrib da isha'i tayi tadanci abinci sannan tasha magani tabi lfyar gado.
Kasancewar a agajiye take bata wani Dade a kwance ba barci ya sadado ya dauke ta...✍

042





Washegari tunda tayi sallar asuba bata koma barciba.

Laptop dinta taja tadanyi yan dube dube da gyare gyare akan abinda yashafi bakery dinta da ice cream joint.

Ciwon jikin yarage sosai saidai haryanzu yatsunta na zugi saboda typing datayi.


Qarfe bakwai da Rabi ta rufe laptop din, ta tashi ta jona ruwa a electric kettle sannan tashiga wanka.

Bata jimaba sosai tafito ta shirya cikin atamfa Riga da skirt ta Dora baqar after dress ta yane kanta da gyalen after dress din.

Yauma bawani kwalliya tayiba tadai dan bursuna powder da kajal ta taje lashes din idanunta da mascara.

Hada kakkauran shayi tayi ta zauna tasha sannan ta feshe jikinta da turare tasaka takalmi tadau Jakarta tafice.


Direct parking space tanufa nan taga duka motocinshi nanan alamun be fitoba.

Shigewa motarta tayi tabata wuta sannan tafice daga gidan.



Qarfe 8:25am ta isa company din.

Parking tayi a space din sannan tafito cikin unique shigarta ta wuce cikin company din cikin takunta mai cikeda nutsuwa.



A gyare ta tarda office dinta sai tashin qamshi yake da alama ma ba'a jima da gyarashi ba.

Babu 6ata lokaci ta jawo aikin da bata idaba jiya tahauyi.

Cikin qanqanin lokaci tagama sannan tadawo ta zauna gaban system dinta ta bude.


Sai qarfe goma Ashraf ya iso company din.

Ta gaban office dinta yazo yawuce amma ko daga kai ta kalleshi batayiba hasalima nunawa tayi batama lura dashiba.


Saida tagama abinda tajeyi tsaff sannan ta kwashi dukan takardun tafito daidai shima sadeeq yafito daga office dinshi.

Ganin tana niyyar yin fuska tawuce yasashi saurin cewa

"Good morning ma'am"

Tsayawa tayi batareda ta juyoba, tasan ita yakamata ta gaidashi sbd yafita matsayi a company din amma batajin tana iya gaidashi, a halin yanzu ta tsani duk Wanda keda alaqa da A.A idan aka cire Ummy da baby.

"Hyy" kawai tace zata wuce.

"Yau za'ayi meeting dinnan ko?" Yaqara fada 

Batareda ta tsaya daga tafiyar datakeba tace
"Nasani"

Tayi knocking sau daya tabude kofar tashige tabarshi anan.


Jin anbude kofar anshigo yasashi dago kai yana kallonta.

Qarasowa tayi gabanshi batareda tabari sun hada idanu ba ta ajiye takardun kan desk din.

"Good morning" tafada ciki ciki

Be amsaba kuma bebar kallonta ba

"Ga papers dinnan, kuma yau munada meeting biyu, daya qarfe 12:00pm dayan kuma bayan asr"

Bece mata komai ba sai jawo takardun data ajiye yayi yafara dubawa.

Yayi mammaki sosai na ganin ta gama aikin duka kamar yanzu, shi bemayi tunanin zata gamashi yau ba, a tunaninshi saikuma batun gobe.

Be bari mammakin ya bayyana a fuskarshi ba ya cigaba da dubawa ko zaiga mistake ko dayane amma komai daidai yake kuma cikin tsari.

"Ok, amshi" yafada yana miqamata takardun.

Babu musu ta amsa

"Ki chikwikwiyesu duka"

Dum  gabanta yafadi tayi saurin dagowa ta kalleshi.

Dagamata gira daya yayi yace
"Yes, squeeze it"

Wani Abu ta hadiye a maqoshinta dakyar sannan ta ajiyesu kan table din ta fara dauka da daya daya tana chukwikwiyewa tana ajiyewa gefe.

Tasan yayi hakanne don ya 6atamata rai yaganta cikin bakinciki saidai bazata bashi abinda yakeso ba don haka ko afuska bata nuna ta damuba, fuskarta nanan dai yadda take babu yabo babu fallasa amma karka bincika zuciyar.


Haka taita chukwikwiyewa harta gama.

"Sasu a waste basket"

Babu musu ta kwashesu ta zubasu a wani emptyn kwadon shara dake daga can gefe.


"Good ga wannan ki karanta" yafada yana miqamata wata paper

Amsa tayi tana dubawa

"Ba aciki zaki karanta ba, a bayyane"

Daidaita muryarta tayi sannan tafara karantawa.

" 1. Lokacin zuwa office 8:00am

2. Hada coffee 8:55am

3. Gabatarda aikin da aka kwana dasu 9:10am

4. Girmama na gaba dakai ta hanyar kiranshi sir ko ma'am

5. Kar ashigo office harsai anbada izini duk jimawarka kana knocking.

6. Another coffee 3:00pm

7. Closing time 6:30pm"

Dago kai tayi daga takardar bayan tagama karantawa.

Ahankali yabude bakinshi kamar beso yawani yi balancing a kujera yana dan jujjuyawa yace

"Nakine.. Fatan za'a kiyaye"

"Ok" tafada a ataqaice

"Ok..what?" Yafada yana tsareta da idanu

Banza tayi dashi don batajin tana iya kiranshi da sir din dayakeso, Kai ina? Bekaiba.

"Magana Nike"

Nanma tsit don ko gefenshi bata kallaba

Murmushi mai dan sauti yasaki sannan yajawo  wasu takardun cikin wadanda yabata jiya ya Diba da yawa Suma batareda yasan adadinsu ba ya tura a gabanta yace
"Same thing da kikayi jiya" ya koma ya jingina da kujerar yana kallonta.

Babu musu ta kwasa har gyara zamansu take kamar bata damuba sannan tajuya tafice.

Binta da kallo yayi harta fice sannan yayi qwafa yana jinjina kai.



Komawa tayi office dinta ta Dora takardun saman desk ta zauna kan kujera ta kifa kan akan desk din tana sauraron yadda zuciyarta ke bugawa kamar zata fado Gawani suya na musanmman datakeyi.

So take tayi kuka ko zataji sauqi amma kwata kwata kukan yaqi zuwa, ambaton sunan Allah tafarayi tana dan jujjuya kanta saman desk din.

Ta jima ahakan sannan tafarajin sauqi acikin zuciyarta.

Tashi tayi ta jawo papers din Suma tahau copy dinsu.



11:55am ta dakatar da aikin datake ta miqe tanufi office din A.A don 12 dot za'ayi meeting din.

Kwankwasawa tayi taji shiru tasake nanma shiru, tasake nanma tsit.

Murmushin takaici tasaki, wato don ya wulaqanta ta yasashi kafa dokar idan ba iziniba aka badaba kar a shiga.

Komawa tayi office din ta share shi, ayi cancelling din meeting din for all she care.

12 daidai sadeeq yafito daga office dinshi da niyyar wucewa shima meeting din.

Mammaki yayi ganin saudart a office tana aikin ta ta dode kunne da earphones irin Wanda ake dorawa akai dinnan.

To ko batasan da ita za'ayi meeting din ba ne?
Tambayar dayayiwa kanshi kenan.

Qarasowa office din yayi yayi knocking.

Dagowa tayi ta kalleshi batareda tace komai ba.

Shigowa yayi ya tsaya daga bakin kofa yace

"Are you not supposed to be in the meeting Hall?"

Dan zame earphones din kunnenta tayi tana cewa "Perdon?"

Ajiyar zuciya yayi yace "nace meyasa baki fito meeting din ba?"

"Boss dinne ke barci" tafada tana maida earphones dinta 

Shiru yayi cikin mammaki.

"Barci?"

Bata ko dagoba bare yasamu amsa.

Fita yayi ya nufi office din A.A din ya bude batareda ya kwankwasa ba.


A.A daya cika faam saboda tafiyarta datayi daga tayi knocking uku be amsaba kuma gashi har sha biyun ta gota bata dawoba ya dago Kai don ganin wane isashen ke shigowa batareda knocking ba. 

Ganin sadeeq ne yasashi kauda kai.

Shima sadeeq qara tamke fuska yayi don haryanzu be huceba ya qaraso ciki.

"Cancel it" yafada batareda ya kalleshi ba.

"Am not speaking Chinese" inji Ashraf yana wullamashi mugun kallo

Banza Ashraf yayi ya kyalleshi 

"Look Ashraf idan saboda saudart ne fine, ka sallameta din, atleast kasan badakai ta dogaraba kuma itama Kanta bada son ranta take aikinnanba ni shaidane, zanje inyi firing dinta kowama ya huta" yafada afusace yanufi kofa.

"Don't dare me! Ban sakaba"

"Saika sani?"

"Sadeeq don't!"

Hakan yasashi juyowa yana kallonshi

"Menene to? Bakai kace kayi firing dinta ba?"

"That was then, amma yanzu dolene tayi aikin, dolene!"

"Kai ka isa kasata dolene?"

"Namayi yawa so shut the hell up!"

"Mtcheew yanzu zaka meeting din ne koko?"

"Dole saina jera dakai?"

Tsaki sadeeq yaja yafice yana fadin "kanka yakeji"


Koda yafita bega saudart a office din ba hakan yasashi wucewa Hall fin meeting din inda a can yaganta sunadan tattaunawa da baqin cikin Sakin fuska.

Saida ya mula yasha iska sannan yashigo Hall din fuskarshi a tamke.

Saida ya zauna sannan meeting din yafara.


Saudart ce ta miqe tafara gabatar da dalilin taruwar meeting din.

Sosai ta burge mutane da yanayin yadda take gabatar da abin cikin nutsuwa da turancinta lafiyayye ga fuskarta a sake very friendly, hakan yasa kowa ya maida hankalinshi kacokan akanta.

Bayan tagama takoma ta zauna nan P.A wato sadeeq ta Dora daga inda ta tsaya yana yimusu bayani dalla dalla akan abinda ya tarasu sannan shima boss ya Dora da nashi shima cikin bi daki daki da ganin cewa ya warware musu komai.


Ataqaice dai saida sukayi awa daya a office din sannan aka gama meeting din kuma alhamdullilah ansamu abinda akeso Gawani farijinin da saudart tayi nan take don sai yabonta ake kan qwarewarta da fara'arta.

Koda suka fito direct office dinta takoma tayi azahar sannan takoma kan aikinta dukda tasan shima qarshen shi basket za'a sakasu.

Uku dot ta dakata ta tashi tana gyara gyalenta sannan tafito ta nufi office dinshi don hadamashi coffee din.


Bugu daya, biyu, uku amma yanzu ma tsit ba'ada niyyar amsawa hakan yasata Jan tsaki ta murda kofar tashiga da sallama...✍

043




Yanzuma dagowa yayi yana kallonta, batareda tabari sun hada idanu ba ta nufi coffee maker din office din tafara hadawa.


Dauke Kai yayi ya maida kan rubutun dayake acikin zuciyarshi kuma yana ayyana yadda zai koyamata hankali.

Wato simple instruction bazata biba, kenan she's too big tajira yabata izinin shigowa?

Kwafa yayi cikin zuciyarshi, he wonder why she's so proud of herself, jin kanta yayi yawa, me take dashi? Metake taqama dashi?

Idan kyau ne akwai wadanda suka dameta suka shanye a kyau suna binshi, akwai classic ladies dirarri wadanda saita raina kanta agabansu masu so ko kallo daya ne yayimasu amma basu isheshi kalloba.

Mace bata ta6a rainashi ba yadda ta rainashi, mace bata ta6a nuna halin ko-in-kula dashiba kamar yadda takeyi, wasu ma dying suke dan suji ya furta koda kalma dayace garesu amma this one is as if ko ganinshi batason yi.

Babu musu tasake hada wani takawo ta ajiye.

Gyara fuskarta tayi yakoma normal sannan ta fita.

Yanzu ma alhamdullilah the meeting is successful and saudart is becoming more popular, tana wani baiwa na shiga rai farat daya don haka nan danan tasiye zuciyar mutane dayawa.

Sosai suke yabonta don wasu saida suka magantu suna cema Ashraf wannan tafi wancan don Helen babu abinda ta iya sai shegen iyayi, a maqe murya ana rangwada , gata kullum a tsuke kuma irin matan nanne masu ga6a ga6an jiki, shiyasa wani sa'in idan tasa wasu kayan maimakon ta burge saima tazama abun kallo.

6:30pm tabar office din kamar yadda yafada.

A ataqaice dai haka saudart taita fama, mugunta kala kala A.A kemata, duk yadda zai 6atamata rai saiya yi, haka kawai zai sata unnecessary Abu daga qarshe yasata yagewa ko lallatawa da kanta, hakan ba qaramin 6atamata rai yakeba hakannan take daurewa don shima ta gumamashi.

Sai yanzu tagane dalilin dayasa baby ke kiranshi mugu don yaci sunan kuwa, don kusan kullum saita la6e toilet tasha kukanta.

A bangaren daddy kuwa yashiga damuwa sosai, tun lokacin databar office dinshi yashiga damuwa, yasan be kyauta mataba Sam, yasan yaso kanshi dayawa, rabon daya ganta kosuyi waya tun ranar, ita bata kiraba shikuma kunya ta hanashi kira.


Addadafe ranakun satin suka wuce aka shiga weekend.

Sai a lokacin tasamu damar leqa bakery dinta da ice cream joint. Kuma babu laifi Allah yasamata albarka a harkar don tana samu sosai.

Ranar lahadi kuwa qannenta sukazo suka yimata yini, sosai taji dadin zuwansu don sun debemata kewa sosai, basu suka koma gidaba sai magrib bayan ta cikasu da gift sosai.

Suna tafiya itama ta hayewarta sama don batason ganinshi, rabonta dashi tun ranar Friday a office kuma batason ganinshi din sai goben shima don yazama dolene don yanzu tsanarshi qara farashi take kowacce daqiqa mai tafiya...✍

044



 MONDAY

jiki a sanyaye take shiri.tana tunanin ya kuma haduwarsu ta yau zata kasance.

Idan akwai abinda tafi tsana yanzu to bewuce ganin koda wulginshine ba, gani take kamar kullum qaramata tsanarshi ake, tasan yauma dakyar idan bazai sata kukaba.

Qarfe 8:00am daidai yayimata a office, tunda kuma tashigo tashiga busy 

Abu guda dazai burgeka gameda ita shine duk tsanarshi da aikin datake hakan be hanata yin aikinta tsakani da Allah, she's so hardworking shima shaidane.

Be shigowa company din ba sai wajajen 9:00am, kamar kullum bata nuna taganshi ba harya shige office.

Can taji landline dinta na ringing, batareda ta dauke kai daga abinda takeyi ba ta daga wayar ta kara a kunne.

"Come" taji ance aka katse kiran.

Bin wayar tayi da kallo sannan ta saki tsaki ta ajiye ta tashi

Kamar dai yadda tasaba knocking uku tayi bata jira amsaba tashiga

"Good morning" be amsata ba yace

"Have a seat" batareda ya kalleta ba.

Jan kujerar gaban table dinshi tayi ta zauna.


Shiru yadan ratsa office din nawani lokaci kanshi kasa yana yan rubuce rubuce kafin ya dago ya kalleta.

Sanye take da dakkakiyar shadda dark purple sai farin gyalen data yafa stylishly fuskar kamar kullum babu tarkacen makeup. Sosai tayi kyau in her own way.

Daddy?

Addu'o'i sukayi mata sosai da shawarwari nagari sai la'asar tabar gidan tawuce mall din daddy.

Dariya taita yimata daddy ganin sai kakkauda kai yake wai besan su hada ido.

Tun yana kunyarta harya ware sukaita fira don saudart bata wani dauki abun dazafi ba yadda yayi tunani.
Sai tambayarta yake ya A.A ke treating dinta sai tace lfy, beyimata komai.

Matsamata yayi akan tayi shopping na tafiya.

Dafarko taqiya amma daya matsamata saita dan tsinci gowns kadan.
Ganin haka yasa Dad yimata shopping din dakanshi, gowns yan kanti ya kwasanmata kala kala kowanne da March na shoes da bag dinshi.

Sosai taita complaining sunyi yawa amma shi ko a jikin shi Shidai burinshi ya faranta mata.

Ba ita tadawo gidaba sai wajajen 9:00pm shima daddy ya kawota dakanshi.

Fitowa tayi tana dagamashi hannu harya wuce, she's so happy, duk saita nemi baqincikinta ta rasa.

Haka tashigo gidan niqi niqi da kaya, tun a parking space tagane yana gidan.

Da sallama tashiga falon, hangenshi tayi kan daya daga cikin cushion din falon ,zaune sanye da baqar singlet da baqin wando ya duqufa kan laptop.

Kallo daya sukayima juna suka kauda kai.

Wuce shi tayi ta hayewarta sama batareda tasake kallonshi ba tashige daki

Toilet tawuce tayi wanka don ta kwashi gajiya sosai.
Koda tafito shirya wa tayi cikin kayan barci sannan tahau shirya kayanta.

Saida ta tabbatar ta kammala komai sannan tabi lfyr gado ta kwanta tana sauke ajiyar zuciya...✍

"Well bansanshi ba, bansan ya biyaba, abinda nasani shine nayi shopping and am paying myself" tafada cikin turanci...✍

047




"Erm.. Am sorry ma'am amma anbiya" Matar tafada.

(Note duk da turanci suke magana ni zan dan sirka da Hausa saboda sauqin fahimta)

"Then zan maida kayan" tafada tana qoqarin juyawa.

A halin yanzu babu abinda ta tsana kamar ayimata alfarma, alfarmar ma ta rasa Wanda zaimata sai A.A? No, bata ciba yamata gori inaga taci?

"Please ma'am, wait a minute" inji Matar tana yan latse latse a landline din gabanta sannan ta dauka ta kara a kunne.

Magana tafara cikin yaren Spanish, itadai saudart shiru tayi tana sauraronta dukda batasan me take cewaba.

Can saita ajiye wayar murmushi a fuskarta tace "ok ma'am, kawo ATM din"

Babu musu ta miqamata tacire kudin sannan ta maido mata.


A bangaren Ashraf kuwa duk abinda yafaru yana sane don suna tareda managern supermarket din daya kasance tsohon abokinshi ne tun primary.

Agabanshi Matar takira manajan tana cemashi Matar tayi insisting kan ita zata biya kudin

Jin haka yasa manajan gayama Ashraf din, nunawa yayi babu matsala amma deep down kamar yayi bindiga yaji don a gurinshi ba qaramin zubda mashi mutunci tayi most especially da manajan ke tsokanarshi wai ya canza dubara wannan batayi aiki ba don duk tunaninshi irin yaganta dinnan ne ya qyasa yana son shigar da kanshi.

Shidai banza yayi dashi sukayi sallama sannan yanufi motarshi daidai itama ta qaraso.

Beko kalleta ba ya bude mazaunin driver yashiga, cikin zuciyarshi yana ayyana abinda zaimata ya huce.

Oho batasan yanayiba, itama budewa tayi ta zauna sannan yaja kamar zasu tashi sama sukabar wajen.

Yadda sukazo haka suka koma babu mai cewa komai.

So take ta tambayeshi inda ake siyarda layi amma tana gudun dizgi don taga fuskarshi babu alamun yakosan Kalmar dariya, hakan yasa tashafawa kanta lfy tayi shiru har suka iso gida.

Yana parking ta bude kofar kamar dama jira take tafita hannunta riqeda ledojinta, zata wuce ya dakatar daita dacewa

"Gobe 10:00am.. Be ready" yafada ataqaice.

Batace komaiba tajuya tashige tana ta6e baki.

Saida ajiye duk abubuwan data siyo inda ya kamata sannan ta jona ruwan shayi a heater data siyo ta shige toilet don yin wanka.

Kayan barci tasa bayan ta fito ta hada kakkauran shayi da kayan tea din data siyo tasha sannan ta shige cikin bargo sai 😴



Washegari tunda wuri ta shirya don sosai take bama lokaci muhinmmanci, idan aka bata appointment bata wucewa saida dalili, batada African time ko kadan

Tun tana jira adaki tana kasa kunnen jin fitowarshi harta fito falo ta zauna ta cigaba da jiranshi.

Sanye take cikin wata baqar Dubai gown Wanda yad'an kamata daga sama ya bude daga qasa. Tayi rolling da gyalen rigar ta Dora qatuwar rigar sanyi baqa akai mai flowers farare jefi jefi.

Kafarta sanye da baqin booth na mata Wanda yakai mata har gwiwa, fuskarta daukeda simple makeup, Jan la66anta sai walqiyar lip gloss suke, tayi kyau sosai cikin shigar abinka da farar fata.

Fiddo hannunta na dama  dake cikin aljihun rigar sanyin tayi ta kalli baqar agogon dake daure da tsintsiyar hannunta taga har sha daya da minti goma.

Sake kallon kofar dakinshi tayi a karo na ba adadi tanajin kamar taje ta bubbuga kofar.

Tsaki taja cikin jin haushi, ita ba komai yasa ta qagara yafito sutafi ba saidan sotake sufita ta siya sim card tasa kozataji muryar yan gida taji sanyi.


Maida kanta tayi kan jikin kujerar, hannunta zube cikin aljihun rigar sanyin, zuciyarta ba suya.

Wannan wane irin wulaqanci ne? Yace 10:00am gashi har to 12 amma ko niyyar fitowa be dashi.



Shikau a bangarenshi  yana sane daita kawai wulaqanci ne, acewarshi itama taji yadda yaji jiya a supermarket. Tundazu yana jin motsinta a falo yayi biris ya qyaleta.

Sai 11:20 ya tashi yashiga wanka bayan yan mintuna yafito sannan yafara shiryawa don qarfe 2;00pm sukeda meeting din daya kawosu.

Cikin farin suit mai Jan shirt daga ciki ya shirya, yasa necktie ja irin dan guntun nan, ya taje sumar kanshi daketa walqiya saboda gyara sannan ya feshe Jikinshi da turare sannan ya dauki briefcase dinshi ya fito.


Afalo ya isketa lafe jikin kujera idanunta a lumshe Amma yasan ba barci take ba, kallo daya yayimata ya dauke kai cikin basarwa yana gyara necktie dinshi.

Taji fitowarshi amma taqi bude idanu don iya shaqa ta shaqa.

"Coffee" yafada in his usual husky voice

Saurin bude idanu tayi tana kallonshi cikin mammaki, she was like, what the hell?

Shikau babu abinda yadameshi ya duqufa sai gyara takalminshi yake.

Ganin bata tashi ba yasashi dagowa yana kallonta, sai yaga itama shi take kallo fuskarnan har wani ja ja take don 6acin rai, abinda ta Dade yanaso kenan, ya 6atamata rai.

"Hello??" Yafada yana waving hannu a fuskarta

"Nace coffee and fried spiced egg" yafada cikin son qara qular daita

"What? Ni kuku ce?" Tafada cikin tsananin fishi don yau kwata kwata takasa controlling din fushin ta

"Then mecece? Am your boss kuma komai bazaki sai kinyi it's part of your job, after all biyanki zanyi ba kyauta bane" yafada Yanajin wani nishadi a zuciyarshi ganin sai qara hawa take

"Yes aiki nake maka but am not a cook, am a secretary for crying out loud" tafada tana yarfa hannuwa cikin fishi.

"Wannan ke ya shafa, nidai kawomin abinda nasaki, now!" Ya qarasa maganar cikin dan daga murya


Shiru tayi ranta a mugun 6ace, tunda take bata ta6a shiga 6acin rai data kasa controlling irin yau ba.

Ya shanyata na kusan 2hours sannan kuma yace ta hadamashi coffee harda wata shegiyar fried spiced egg?


Dakyar ta iya controlling din kanta sannan ta tashi fuu tashiga kitchen.

Binta yayi ta kallo harta shige sannan ya juyo yana murmushin jindadi


Cikin yan mintuna saigashi ta dawo riqeda mug din coffee ta diremashi a gabanshi tanufi hanyar dakinta a fusace

"Karki qara step guda anan" yafada yana dakatar daita.

"Kijirani ingama mutafi" yafada yana daukar mug din batareda yayi complaining din Rashin ganin kwan ba.

Nanma saida ya 6atamusu lokaci sannan ya gama sha ya miqe yayi gaba yana cewa "shall we"

Binshi tayi da mugun kallo sannan itama ta biyo bayanshi zuciyarta kamar zatayi bindiga.


Saida yashiga mota ya zauna sannan tafito.

Tunda tafito yake kallonta tacikin motar.

Ta taho sanye da fuskar angry bird yan kumatunta sun dan turo alamun she's still angry.

Tunda yake beta6a ganin Wanda fushi yaima kyau ba kamarta, kamar fuskar taita zama ahakan.

Ganin ta qaraso yasashi saurin kauda kai yana basarwa.

Bude kofar tayi ta shigo ta zauna still fuskarta a tamke jitake kamar taita ihu don haushi.

Kunna motar yayi yaja suka fita daga harabar gidan.

Tsit motar tayi kowa da abinda yasha mishi kai, saudart sai cika take tana batsewa, jitake kamar tayi kuka, sosai take missing yan Niger she badly want to call them.

"The meeting will hold at 2:00pm" taji yafada

Yaitayi kamar bata jishiba don ko kallon gefenshi batayiba.

Hakan yasashi juyowa yace
"Are you deaf?" Ya tambaya cikin husky voice

Juyowa tayi ta watsa mashi Lulu eyes dinta sannan ta dauke kai tana cewa "ok"

Shiru yayi shima ya kauda Kai yana lumshe ido yana budewa ahankali don shikadai yasan abinda yaji data watsamashi idanun nan.

Cigaba da tuqin yayi yana sauraron bugun zuciyarshi data sauya a take.

Itakau cigaba da kallon waje tayi tana kumburi gashi tana son cemashi ya biya dasu wajen saida layi amma takasa.


Kamar wasa sai gani tayi yayi parking gaban wani babban shagon siyarda wayoyi.

Hakan yasata saurin gyara zamanta daga kishingiden datake tana kallon wajen murmushi na su6ucemata batareda tasaniba.

Jin kamar ana kallonta yasata juyowa suka hada idanu, yawani basar ta hanyar gallamata harara yana ta6e baki.

Kauda Kai tayi tana cewa "oho dai" cikin zuciyarta amma qasan zuciyarta fall farinciki at last zata samu kiransu daddy

Saida tabari yafita sannan itama tafito lokacin harya shigewarshi, hakan yasa itama ta shiga zuciyarta fall murna

Direct wajen wani saurayi taje cikin masu saida wayoyin shagon

"Hi" tafada 

"Hello ma'am you're welcome, wane taimako zan iya yimiki?" Yafada cikin murmushi

"Layi nakeso" duk a harshen turanci suke maganar

Nan ya fiddomata ta sayi guda biyu tasaka nan take

"Zai fara aiki bayan awa daya" yafada mata yana bata receipt

"Ok thanks" tafada tana amsa fuskarta fall murna


Waje tafita fuskarta a sake sa6anin dazu ta taddashi jingine da motar ya rungume hannu a qirji.

Qarasowa tayi ahankali zata zagaya ya dakatar daita da "take" yana cillomata makullan motar.

Cafewa tayi tana kallonshi da alamun tambaya

"Drive us ai ba nikadai na iya driving ba" yafada yana zagayawa inda take zama

Mere baki tayi sannan tadawo ta bude mazaunin driver tashiga ta kunna motar sannan tajasu cikin driving dinta mai burgewa.

Tafiya suka fara yana gwada mata hanya har suka iso wani shahararre kuma qawattacen hotel.

"Ok shiga" yafada yana danne dannenshi.

Dan jimm  tayi kamar zatayi magana saikuma tafasa ta shiga ta samu wuri a parking lot tayi parking.

Fitowa sukayi kusan tare suna kallon environment din.

Jin ana kabbara yasashi basu umarnin sufara sallah sannan.

Masjid din hotel din suka shiga shi bangaren maza ita na mata don yin sallar.

Koda aka gama sallar tayi addu'o'inta saita fito.

Hangoshi tayi da wasu mutane uku duk cikin shigar suit, biyu farare daya baqi suna magana da alama sune zasuyi meeting din dasu.

Qarasowa tayi wajen cikin Sakin fuska tana gaishesu suna amsawa Suma cikin fara'a

"Meet my secretary, Miss saudart shamsu" inji Ashraf yana nunata

"Nice meeting you miss" suka hada baki wajen fadin haka.

"My pleasure sir(s)" tafada cikin girmamawa

"Shall we?" Inji baqin cikin mutanen yana nuna hanyar ciki.

"Sure" duk sukace gabadaya suka dunguma suka shiga ciki suna tafiya suna fira jefi jefi...✍

048



Restaurant din hotel din sukayi reserving don gudanar da meeting din.


Zauna suka kan kujerun dake zagayeda wani round table, kowanne da robar swan a gabanshi da glass cup duk sunyi shiru suna sauraron bayyañin da daga daga cikin mutanen mai suna *Hussain* keyi.


Meeting ne akan wani contract na ordern gwalagwalai dazasuyi, kasancewar companyn A.A companine na dealer gwalagwalai da zinarai, yana daya daga cikin companyn dayayi fice a Nigeria dama Africa gabadaya, yana ordering din gwalagwalai a qasashe daban daban.


To anan ma hakan take, zuwa yayi don yin ordern wasu latest design na gwalagwalan masu tsadan gaske don sabbin design ne don ba'a gama saninsu a duniya ba.


Wani qaramin akwatin glass ne a tsakiyar table din Wanda ke dauke da sample din gold din.

Saida Hussain yagama 6a66atunshi sannan ya buqaci su duba suga ingancinshi.

Budewa baqin cikinsu yayi ya fiddo  ya miqama saudart dake gefen Ashraf, ta amsa sannan ta miqama Ashraf.

Sundan Dade suna dubawa (Ashraf & saudart) suna jujjuyawa suna dan qus qus tsakaninsu da alamun shawara suke yankewa.

Sudai mutanen kallonsu suke har suka gama sannan Ashraf ya maidama saudart Itakuma ta miqama Wanda yabata.

Cikin inganttaciyar turancinta tace

"Yayi kyau sosai, amma kunzo mana da kala kalan designs dinsu ne, munason mu za6a" tafada tana kallonsu, Ashraf dake gefenta na kada kai alamun abinda tafada gaskiya ne

Baqin Wanda yakira kanshi da *zahid* yace

" sosaima, gashi Ku za6a" yafada yana bude musu laptop ya shiga hotunansu sannan ya turomusu Gabansu.

Nan suka shiga dubawa suna za6an choice dinsu suna qus qus, idan ka gansu a lokacin baka ta6a tunanin tom & jerry dinnan ne don dukansu sunci serious sosai.

Saida suka za6i iya Wanda sukeso sannan aka maida musu laptop din.

Nan sukayi cinikin iya adadin dazasu saya Wanda za'a turomusu ta jirgin ruwa bisa yarjejeniyar zasu fara bada Rabin kudin anan, Rabin kuma sai kaya sun isa.

Anan aka yanke shawarar zasu sake haduwa a companyn su Hussain din ranar Monday don biyan Rabin kudin kamar yadda suka tsara sannan suyi abun a rubuce kowa yasa hannu saboda yazama shaida.


Awa daya meeting din ya dauke su sannan su saudart suka miqe don tafiya kowanne fuskarshi fall fara'a.

Har mota suka rakasu, dayake makullan motar na hannun saudart sai kawai tashiga mazaunin driver ta zauna tana jiran Ashraf dahar yanzu suke magana da mutanen.
 Can sukayi musabaha sannan shima yashiga motar suka bar hotel din.


Tunda suka hau hanya babu Wanda yacewa kowa uffan gar suka qarasa gida.

Lokacin da suka iso har anfara kiraye kirayen sallar la'asar don haka bema shiga gidanba yawuce masjid din estate din Itakuma ta shigewarta ciki don gabatarda tata.

Bayan tagama sallar ne taciro wayarta tafara kiran yan Niger.

Da daddy tafara, sosai suka sha fira dashi Wanda Rabi shagwa6a ce take zuba mashi yana biyemata sannan takira mamy nan Suma suka gaisa da kowa na gidan kowanne nabata sabtun tsarabar dazatayi mashi sai dariya take musu.

Sai bayan sunyi sallama sannan ta bugama Ummy.

Sosai Ummy taji dadin kiran nata, sunsha fira sosai kafin takaima baby wayar

As usual ihun nan nata na hauka taitayi da sunan murna, nan sukasha fira kamar ba gobe sai tsokanarta baby take wai ya? An samu tsarabar nata koko da saura? Itakuma tana amsa mata da zata gane kuranta ne saita gayamashi.

Haka sukaita firarsu, dakyar suka ajiye wayar kowanne najin qaunar dan uwanshi har cikin zuciyarshi.



***********************************

Tana cikin shirin kwanciya kasancewar har Tara tayi taji ana bubbuga kofarta.

Dan jimm tayi daga gyaran zanen gadon datake ta kalli kofar.

Jin ansake bugowa yasata Sakin bedsheet din ta zura hijabin sallarta akan doguwar rigar barcinta sannan tanufi kofar.


Tana budewa taga shine, gyara tsayuwarta tayi tana kallonshi da alamar tambaya.

"Coffee.. Kikawomin a study room" yafada yana wucewa.


Galala tabishi da kallo harya shige.

Mene? Coffee cikin Daren nan? Wannan wane irin wahalarwa ne?
Mutum na shirin barci awani tsiromashi aikin hada coffee? 

Sosai ranta ya 6aci don barci ke idanunta burinta kawai ta kwanta.

Babu yadda ta iya haka tawuce kitchen din ranta a jagule, tsaki kau tafishi yafi cikin kwando kafin tagama hadawa.

A study room din tasameshi zaune gaban laptop sai danne danne yakeyi.

Ciki ciki tayi sallama sannan ta qaraso gabanshi kamar bataso sannan ta dungure mashi mug din coffeen a kan table din gabanshi tajuya da niyyar komawa.

"Come back here" yafada batareda ya dago daga kan laptop din ba.

Saida tayi jimm kaman bazata juyoba sannan tajuyo tadawo gabanshi ta tsaya.

Dagowa yayi yana kallon yadda taketa faman kumburi tawani tsaya mashi akai.

"Da ina zaki?" Ya tambayeta 

"Ina bayan dakina?" Tafada cikin son danne fushinta

"Na sallameki ne?" Ya fada cikin son qular daita


"Ba na hada cofeen ba?  Ni Am sleepy wlh" tafada tana turo baki.

"Barci? Dama barci ya kawoki nan?"

"Bashi ya kawoni ba, amma ai yanzu na hadamaka coffee din ko? Zan iya tafiya ko?" Tafada cikin tsiwa tsiwa

Daukar mug din cofeen yayi ya kafa Kai ya shanye sannan ya diremata 

"Make another one"

Wani Abu taji ta taso ya toshe mata maqoshi, Kutt...

"Bakijiba? Nace ki hado wani" tafada yana kallon yadda fuskarta ke yin ja ja ja ja alamun tana cikin tsananin 6acin rai.

Batace komai ba ta figi mug din ta fice tana bugomashi kofa har yana toshe kunne.
Binta yayi da kallo sannan ya jinjina Kai yana murmushi

"Shima wannan you'll pay for it" yafada yana maida hankalinshi kan laptop din.


Can saigata ta dawo ta qara dungure mashi mug din har coffee din badan zubewa.

Dagowa yayi yana kallonta da mammaki

"Wai kwakwalki qalau kuwa?"

'Kai ka cancanci tambayar' tafada a zuciyarta

Banza tayi dashi ta juyamashi qeya.

Qwafa yayi ya cigaba da danne dannenshi sannan ya dauki mug din yakai baki da niyyar kur6a.

Kur6a daya yayi yayi saurin furzoshi ko maqoshi be kaiba saboda wani zau dayaji a harshenshi.

Kauda Kai tayi saurin yi tana son hadiye dariyarta

"Kutt... Uban me kika samun a coffee? Kasheni zakiyi?" Ya tambaya yana kallonta cikin mammaki

"Ni me nasa?" Ta tambaya tana dan matsawa baya.

"Me kika sa ko? To wlh saikin shanyeshi yafada yana daukar mug din ya nufota.

Ai a sittin tayi wani turning tana fasa qara ta bude kofar tayi waje tana tsuwa.

Binta shima yayi dagudu saidai kafin ya taddota harta shige daki ta Danna sakata sama da qasa tana numfashi sama sama.


Bubbuga kofar yashiga yi da karfi yana cewa tazo ta bude amma tayi banza dashi saima antayama kofar harara datake

" to wlh ki tabbatar nan zaki cigaba da zama har abada don ido na idonki..."  Sai yayi Kwafa yana jinjina kai sannan yayi tafiyarshi


"Idan na fito karka barni da rai, mugu kawai mummuna" tafada tana murguda baki sannan ta haye gado tashige cikin bargo...✍

Washegari Friday, bata yarda tafito daga dakinta ba saida ta tabbatar yabar gidan gabadaya.

Sai a sannan tasamu kwanciyar hankalin fitowa don yin aikace aikacen datasaba.

Gabanta ne yafadi jin bubbugar kofar abinka da marar gaskiya don duk a tunaninta Ashraf ne.

Kwan ta kashe batareda ya ida soyuwaba ta saka a plate ta jidi kayan breakfast din tayi daki dasu sannan ta dawo cikin sanda ta qaraso kofar tana leqen wajen ta wurin nan na kofa don ganin waye.

Ganin wasu yanmata biyu tsaye yasata Sakin ajiyar zuciya sannan tabude.

Yanmata biyu tagani tsaye fararen fata kowacce tasha kayan sanyinta sai washe mata baki suke.

"Please come in"

"A'a yar uwa, murda ga gidanmu nan kusada ku, bawani tafiya mai tsawo mukayi ba kuma ma sanyi ake ba'a cika shan ruwa ba"

Murmushi saudart tayi sannan ta koma ta zauna tana cewa
"Kenan Ku maqobtanmu ne?"

"Eh mana, fa gidanmu nan No 35 Itakuma wannan No 37" inji Wanda tayi magana dazu

"Wow, nice to meet you" tafada cikin Sakin fuska.

"Thank you, sunana Loveth wannan kuma Reyna" inji mai maganar

"Wow nice name, ni sunana saudart" tafada tana murmushi

"Wow nice name too, amma Ku baqi ne ko?" Inji Wanda aka kira da Reyna

"Eh kwananmu biyu yau" saudart tabasu amsa

"Ayyah ai naganku jiya dazaku fita, banma San akwai mutane saida naganku jiya" inji Loveth

"Ai saboda bamu Dade bane shiyasa" saudart ta amsa

051





Washegari da hantsi tafito daga gidan sanye cikin doguwar hijabi har qasa don ba'a ma hango kayan datasa aciki.

Qarfe sha biyun rana ne amma sai kayi tunanin bakwai din safe ne saboda lullumi dakuma buji.

Direct block *37* tanufa ta kwankwasa kofar gidan.


Shiru taji hakan yasata sake bubbugawa.

"Yes!" Taji anfada daga ciki saikuma taji taku na tunkaro kofar.

Budewa akayi Reyna ta bayyana.

Waro idanu tayi kamar Wanda tayi gamo tana rufe bakinta da tafin hannu.

Harara saudart ta gallamata tana cewa
"To nashigo ne ko naqara gaba?"

Saurin Kamo hannunta Reyna tayi tana cewa
"Oh saudart! Ki shigo, am soo sorry, wlh tun washegari naso nazo amma tsoron shi nake, ina tsoron naje na taddashi ko ya taddani gidan, we're soo sorry!" Tafada tana jawota cikin dakin cikin kulawa.

"Mtcheew, wannan sorry din duk na menene to?" Inji saudart tana kwace hannunta ta nemi kujera ta zauna


Dawowa Reyna tayi kusada ita ta zauna tana cewa
"Wlh tun ranar muka shiga tashin hankali musanmman Amir, gani muke dukanki zaiyi, babu yadda beyi daniba nazo gidanku kona gayamashi block dinku amma tsoro ya hanani don gani nake a yanayinshi dinnan yana iya hadawa damu ya make, am so sorry, hope beyimiki komai ba?" Tafada tana dafa kafadarta.

Tsaki tasake ja tace "ni babu abinda yayimin dalla, ni Abu daban yakawoni kinzo kin isheni da surutu" inji saudart don kwata kwata batason ayi maganar

"Ayyah ai dole na damu ai, haryanzu amir bebar damuna ba, wai inbaki hqr besan ke Matar aure bace"

Dagowa tayi da sauri ta kalleta
"Waya fada miki ni Matar aurece?" Ta tambaya a mammakince

"Amir mana, sun hade da mijin naki yana bashi hqr anan ya fadamashi, ai wlh yanada gaskiya dole ne yayi kishi, imagine wata tazo tace maki tana sonshi kuma the next minute ki gansu tare dole kiji haushi" inji Reyna

Banza saudart tayi ta kyaleta don ita har mancewa take dawani aure dake kanta, jinta take soo free kamar ba Matar aureba.

Ganin zata sake magana tayi saurin katse ta da

"Look Reyna komai yawuce, ninan Abu daban yakawoni, idan kuma bazaki saurareni ba fine"

Saurin riqo hannunta Reyna tayi ganin zata tashi tana cewa
"Ok ok ina jinki, am sorry"

Saida ta murguda mata baki cikin wasa sannan tace
"Gobe zamu koma Nigeria"

Dafe qirji Reyna tayi da sauri kamar Wanda akayima mugun Abu.

"What? Please wasa kike? Nasan wasa kike ko?" Inji Reyna unbelieving

"Hmm wlh dagaske nake, meye abun wasa aciki?"

"Oh My good Lord saudart, akan wannan Abun zaku tafi? Please karku tafi zan kira amir yazo har gida yabaku hqr"

Tsaki saudart taja cikin takaici
"Look nifa nagayamiki nama manta da wannan babin, dama Abu yakawomu kuma mungama shiyasa zamu tafi" tafada tana kallon yadda duk Reyna tabi ta susuce

"No, nasan duk saboda abinda yafaru ne, please don't leave, wlh besan ke Matar aure bace" tafada cikin marairaicewa.

Tsaki saudart taja ta miqe tana cewa 
"Bari kiga intafi tunda bakida ganewa"

Saurin shan gabanta Reyna tayi tana cewa
"Ok ki rantse please, ki rantse ba saboda hakan zaku bar nan ba"

Tsaki saudart taja tace
"Wai nata6a yimiki qarya ne?"

"Nidai please ki rantse"

"To na rantse, mungama abinda yakawomu shiyasa zamu tafi, ke ke tunawa da abinda yafaru ni harna manta, yanzu haka zuwa nayi naji babu inda zaki anjima Ku rakani shopping ke da Loveth?"

Sai a sannan hankalin Reyna ya kwanta har wani sauke ajiyar zuciya tayi

"Better, nazaci sbd haka zaku tafi and maganar shopping? It's capital YES! ko da inda zani bazan bari wannan damar kasancewa dake na qarshe ta su6ucemin ba, waya sani ko bazamu sake ganin junaba?" Tafada tana langwa6a kai gefe

"Insha Allah zamu sake hadewa ok? Koba yanzu ba" tafada itama tana langa6e kai

"I'll miss you" tafada tana rungumeta

"I'll miss you much" inji saudart tana murmushi

Ganin batada niyyar sakinta yasata yimata chakulkuli Wanda hakan yasata saurin sakinta suna dariya tare

"Ok now tafiyar nanan? Loveth zata samu zuwa?"

"Yes, yaushe zamu?"

"4:00pm dot zanzo nan, idan Baku shiryaba zan tafiya ta" tafada cikin kashedi

"Yes ma'am" inji Reyna tana sarawa sukayi dariya gabadaya sannan suka fito tare tayi mata rakiya harta kusan kaiwa gida sannan ta koma





*****************************************


*4:33pm*

"Mtcheew zanyi tafiya ta fa!" Inji saudart dake kofar gidansu Loveth fuskarnan a hade.

Reyna dake gefenta sanye da wando da shirt sai purple jacket ita gwiwa akai gashinta awaje ta kama hannun saudart tana cewa

"Kinga zomu tafi, she's not serious"

Saudart sanye take cikin lace jaa Riga da zani ta yafa gyale baqi stylishly, kallo daya zakamata kasan cikkakiyar bahausa ce.

"Mtcheew mutafi" inji saudart din tana bin Reyna.

Dagudu Loveth tafito daga cikin gidan takalmi a hannu tana cewa

"Kujirani please!"

Saida ta iso motar sannan ta ajiye takalmin tasaka tana numfarfashi wai don tayi Gudu.

Sanye take cikin baqar English gown mai tsaga a baya kanta kuma daukeda hula fara sai qatuwar handbag hannunta.

Haka suka shiga motar Reyna din sunama juna tsiya.

Reyna ce ta zauna mazaunin driver sai saudart gefenta sai Loveth abaya, haka suka tada motar suka bar wajen suka kama hanyar fita daga estate din.







Babu laifi sunyi spending din good time at are, shopping sukayi kamar babu gobe, duk abinda tagani ya burgeta saita dauka.

Haka suka jero suna shopping suna fira da dariya gwanin sha'awa, saida suka gama kaff sannan fa aka bude babin selfie, wai hotunan tarihi.

Sunyi hotuna harna hauka, daga qarshe rasa style din dazasuyi sukayi sai sukaita style din hauka suna dariya, it's a happy moment for them don jisuke kamar karsu dawo gida.


Ataqaice dai sai gab magrib suka baro supermarket din.

Nan suka sako duk kayan dasuka siya a mota suka shiga.

Wannan karon saudart ce ta tuqosu, suna tafe suna tsokanar juna suna dariya.

Koda suka iso gida har angama sallar magrib.

Kofar gidansu saudart suka yada zango don duk tafisu kaya, saida tagama sauke kayanta kaff sannan sukayi sallama akan saisun zo bankwana gobe idan ransu yakai.

Haka ta cicci6i kayan Niki Niki tashiga gidan.




A falo ta ganshi zaune yana danne danne a laptop, kallo daya tamashi ta kauda Kai tawuce shi kayan na rinjayarta.

Binta da kallo yayi harta kai bakin kofarta ta ajiyesu ta bude kofar sannan ta kuma kwasa tayi ciki tarufo kofar.

Ajiyar zuciya ya sauke yana shafa kanshi ahankali sannan ya cigaba da abinda yake.






*********************************

Washegari tunda ta tashi da asuba takasa komawa, dama jiya ba wani barcin kirki tayiba, jitake kamar tajawo lokacin don lokacin be wani yimata Gudu.

Flight din 10:00am garesu amma tun 7:00am take falo zauna sai gyara zama take agogo kau ta dubashi yafi a qilga.


9:00am sai jitayi ana knocking a kofar falon.

Saurin tashi tayi taje ta bude, ihu tasaki ganin Loveth da Reyna ta qanqame su cikin murna

"Hmm muda ba'a ganmu ba saimu juya" inji wata dake baya.

Sai a sannan saudart ta ankare dasu taga sunada yawa ma harda Dr zahra.

Saurin sakinsu tayi tana yi musu iso ciki fuska washe.

Nan suka shigo suka zauna taje ta kawo musu ruwan sha sai washe baki take.

"Hmm sai murna ake za'a gida kamar irin can yafi nan dinnan" inji wata cikinsu

Kamar jira ake nan falo ya kaure da cafta kowa na fadin albarkacin bakinshi itakau Dr sai dariya take musu.


Jin hayaniya a falo yasashi cikin mammaki sosai, to gidan dai babu kayan kallo bare yace kallo aka kunna kuma ma wannan beyi kamada kallo ba yafi jin hayaniyar a zahiri.

Saurin kammala shirin yayi yana duba agogonshi don har Tara da Rabi.


Turus yayi daya fito yaga gugun mutane zaune a falo saudart tsakiyar su suna dariya.

Ganinshi yasasu natsuwa suna gaidashi.

Qarasowa yayi yana amsawa yana kuma gaida Dr.

"Sai Nigeria ko?" Inji Dr zahra cikin tsokana.

Dariya kawai yayi yana shafa kanshi 

"To Allah ya tsare, wish you safe journey, Ku gaishe da mutanen Nigeria, insha Allah zanzo watarana har gidanku, tunda duk munyi exchanging din number" tafada cikin fara'a

"To Allah yasa" inji Ashraf yana satar kallon saudart daketa murmushi.

Farincikin datake aciki afili yake baya 6oyuwa.
At last zasu koma qasarsu.


Fitowa sukayi tareda gungun mutanen sai tsokanarta suke tana biyemasu, har mota suka rakata harda budemata kofa tashiga.

Sai kuma a sannan suka fara marairaicewa wai zasuyi missing juna.

Haka dai suka rabu zuciya babu dadi sai dagawa juna hannu suke har suka bar hangen juna.

Komawa tayi ta jingina da kujerar tana sauke ajiyar zuciya tana murmushi.

Shima dayake satar kallonta tundazu murmushin yasaki ya kauda Kai yana mammakin saurin sabo irin nata, ji yadda mutane sukazo rakiyarsu kamar sunyi shekaru a qasar.


Haka motar tayi tsit har suka qarasa airport din.

Suna fitowa daga motar tafara bin airport din da kallo, kamar jiya ne suka shigo airport dinnan da niyyar shigowa qasar amma wai yau sune aciki da niyyar barin qasar zuwa qasarsu.

"Can't wait" tafada cikin zuciyarta tana murmushi

Saida aka gama komai sannan suka shiga jirgin.

Kamar wancan karon kusada juna suka zauna.

10:00am dot aka fara sannarwa na kowa ya daura belt dinshi.

Wannan karon ba'ayi qauyanci ba nan da nan ta daura.

Jin ana sanarwa na jirgi zai tashi yasa ta koma ta lafe a kujera murmushi a fuskarta.

Jin yafara tafiya yasa bugun zuciyarta qaruwa, jin ya daga yasata Sakin nannauyan ajiyar zuciya

"Bye Madrid, bye Spain" tafada ahankali tana bude idanu tana yiwa qasar kallon qarshe...✍
